### Tizin VOS Translation for ‚ÄúI like apples‚Äù Using Maktay and Zapple

**TASK**: In the fictional language of Tizin, basic sentences are arranged with the Verb first, followed by the direct object, followed by the subject of the sentence. I want to express my love for apples to my Tizin friend.

The word that indicates oneself is "Pa" is the nominative form, "Mato" is the accusative form, and "Sing" is the genitive form.

The root verb that indicates an intense like for something is "Maktay". When it is used in the present, it is used in it's root form, when it is used in the preterit past, it is "Tay", and when it is used in the imperfect past, it is "Aktay". It is used differently than in English, and is better translated as "is pleasing to", meaning that the thing doing the liking is actually the object of the sentence rather than the subject.

The word for apples is borrowed from English in Tizin, and so it is "Apple" is the nominative form, "Zapple" is the accusative form, and "Izapple" is the genitive form.

Please translate "I like apples" to Tizin.

```
{
"role": 'planner',
"plan": '<END>',
"description": "Task completed successfully through direct linguistic analysis. Based on the Tizin grammar rules provided: (1) Sentence structure is Verb-Object-Subject, (2) 'Maktay' means 'is pleasing to' in present tense, (3) The thing being liked (apples) becomes the subject in nominative form 'Apple', (4) The person doing the liking (I) becomes the object in accusative form 'Mato'. Therefore, 'I like apples' translates to 'Maktay Mato Apple' in Tizin. Final answer: Maktay Mato Apple",
}
```

evidence_found.append('Burnley connection')
relevance += 8
print(' üè≠ Burnley connection!')

evidence_found.append('Victorian era reference')
relevance += 6
print(' üèõÔ∏è Victorian era reference!')

# Store findings if relevant

finding = {
'search_number': i,
'result_number': j,
'query': query,
'title': title,
'body': body[:300], # Truncate for storage

}

else:

### Development Step 2: Surrey Lodge History: Victorian Beginnings, Temperance Hall, 1935 Rotating Stage, WWII Bombing, Burnley Relocation

**Description**: Conduct a comprehensive web search to identify Surrey Lodge in South London and trace its historical development during the Victorian era. Focus on finding information about: (1) the original organization that developed Surrey Lodge, (2) its transformation into a temperance hall, (3) the installation of the UK's first rotating stage in 1935, (4) World War II bomb damage, and (5) the company's relocation to Burnley. Use search terms like 'Surrey Lodge South London Victorian era temperance hall', 'first rotating stage UK 1935 temperance hall', 'Surrey Lodge bomb damage World War II Burnley', and 'Victorian temperance organization Surrey Lodge founder'.

**Use Cases**:
- Municipal heritage teams automating extraction of Victorian-era building histories from archived city council websites for preservation grant applications
- Academic history researchers compiling precise timelines of 19th-century social movement venues by analyzing saved HTML search results from digital archives
- Theatre technology historians identifying early rotating stage installations by scanning periodicals and hall websites for 1930s date references
- Insurance risk assessors evaluating wartime bomb damage liabilities by mining online council bomb-damage records and compiled archive pages
- Corporate due diligence analysts tracking legacy company relocations by parsing historical press releases and relocation notices from archived web pages
- Digital librarians structuring metadata on temperance movement meeting halls by extracting organizational founding details from library web archives
- Real estate developers reviewing heritage constraints by retrieving structural transformation records and wartime impact data from municipal HTML archives
- Cultural tourism planners building interactive timelines of historical London landmarks by consolidating extracted event dates and site transformations from saved HTML

html_files = [f for f in os.listdir('workspace') if f.startswith('surrey_lodge_search_') and f.endswith('.html')]
print(f'Found {len(html_files)} Surrey Lodge search result HTML files:')

for i, filename in enumerate(html_files, 1):

print(f' {i}. {filename} ({file_size:,} bytes)')

if not html_files:
print('‚ùå No Surrey Lodge HTML files found - need to re-run searches')
exit()

# Initialize corrected analysis results

'timestamp': '2024-12-19',

print('=' * 80)

# Define key terms with weights for relevance scoring
key_terms = {
'surrey lodge': 10,
'south london': 8,
'temperance': 8,
'temperance hall': 10,
'victorian': 6,
'rotating stage': 10,
'1935': 8,
'first rotating stage': 12,

filepath = os.path.join('workspace', html_file)

# Read HTML content
with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
html_content = f.read()

print(f'File size: {len(html_content):,} characters')

# Parse HTML content - FIXED: Proper variable scope
soup = BeautifulSoup(html_content, 'html.parser')

# Extract text content - FIXED: Ensure page_text is properly defined
page_text = soup.get_text().lower()
print(f'Extracted text: {len(page_text):,} characters')

# Calculate relevance score
found_terms = []
relevance_score = 0

for term, weight in key_terms.items():
if term in page_text:
found_terms.append(term)
relevance_score += weight

print(f'Relevance score: {relevance_score}')
print(f'Found terms ({len(found_terms)}): {', '.join(found_terms[:8])}')

# Extract specific historical indicators
historical_indicators = []

# Look for Surrey Lodge mentions
if 'surrey lodge' in page_text:
historical_indicators.append('Surrey Lodge confirmed')
print('üéØ SURREY LODGE CONFIRMED!')

# Look for temperance hall references
if 'temperance hall' in page_text or ('temperance' in page_text and 'hall' in page_text):
historical_indicators.append('Temperance hall connection found')
print('üèõÔ∏è TEMPERANCE HALL CONNECTION FOUND!')

# Look for rotating stage references
if 'rotating stage' in page_text:
historical_indicators.append('Rotating stage reference found')
print('üé≠ ROTATING STAGE REFERENCE FOUND!')

if '1935' in page_text:
historical_indicators.append('1935 rotating stage date confirmed')
print('üìÖ 1935 DATE CONFIRMED!')

# Look for WWII/bomb damage
if any(term in page_text for term in ['bomb damage', 'bombed', 'war damage', 'blitz']):
historical_indicators.append('WWII damage reference found')
print('üí• WWII DAMAGE REFERENCE FOUND!')

# Look for Burnley connection
if 'burnley' in page_text:
historical_indicators.append('Burnley connection found')
print('üè≠ BURNLEY CONNECTION FOUND!')

# Extract relevant text snippets for context
text_snippets = []
sentences = page_text.split('.')

for sentence in sentences:
sentence = sentence.strip()
if len(sentence) > 20 and len(sentence) < 400:
# Look for sentences containing key terms
if 'surrey lodge' in sentence:
text_snippets.append(sentence)
elif any(term in sentence for term in ['temperance hall', 'rotating stage', 'burnley', '1935']):
text_snippets.append(sentence)

# Remove duplicates and limit
unique_snippets = list(set(text_snippets))[:5]

if unique_snippets:
print(f'Key text snippets found ({len(unique_snippets)}):')
for j, snippet in enumerate(unique_snippets[:3], 1):
print(f' {j}. {snippet[:200]}...')

# Look for dates and timeline information
timeline_info = []
date_patterns = ['1935', '193[0-9]', '19[0-4][0-9]', 'victorian', 'world war', 'wwii']

for sentence in sentences:
sentence = sentence.strip()
if len(sentence) > 15 and len(sentence) < 300:
# Check if sentence contains date-related information
if any(pattern.replace('[0-9]', '') in sentence for pattern in date_patterns):
timeline_info.append(sentence)

# Remove duplicates from timeline info
unique_timeline = list(set(timeline_info))[:3]

# Store analysis results
file_analysis = {
'filename': html_file,
'file_size': len(html_content),
'text_length': len(page_text),
'relevance_score': relevance_score,
'found_terms': found_terms,
'historical_indicators': historical_indicators,
'text_snippets': unique_snippets,
'timeline_information': unique_timeline
}

analysis_results['html_files_analyzed'].append(file_analysis)
analysis_results['historical_findings'].extend(historical_indicators)
analysis_results['timeline_information'].extend(unique_timeline)

# Show high-relevance findings
if relevance_score >= 15 or len(historical_indicators) >= 2:
print(f'üìö HIGH RELEVANCE FINDING - Score: {relevance_score}, Indicators: {len(historical_indicators)}')
elif relevance_score > 0:
print(f'üìù Moderate relevance - Score: {relevance_score}')
else:
print('‚ùå Low relevance - no key terms found')

except Exception as e:
print(f'Error processing {html_file}: {str(e)}')
# Continue with next file instead of stopping
continue

print('\n=== PHASE 3: COMPREHENSIVE EVIDENCE ANALYSIS ===')
print('=' * 80)

total_files = len(analysis_results['html_files_analyzed'])
print(f'Successfully analyzed files: {total_files}')

if total_files > 0:
# Sort files by relevance score
analysis_results['html_files_analyzed'].sort(key=lambda x: x['relevance_score'], reverse=True)

print('\nüìä RELEVANCE RANKING:')
print('-' * 40)

high_relevance = [f for f in analysis_results['html_files_analyzed'] if f['relevance_score'] >= 15]
moderate_relevance = [f for f in analysis_results['html_files_analyzed'] if 5 <= f['relevance_score'] < 15]
low_relevance = [f for f in analysis_results['html_files_analyzed'] if f['relevance_score'] < 5]

print(f'High relevance files (15+ points): {len(high_relevance)}')
print(f'Moderate relevance files (5-14 points): {len(moderate_relevance)}')
print(f'Low relevance files (0-4 points): {len(low_relevance)}')

if high_relevance:
print('\nüéØ TOP HIGH-RELEVANCE FILES:')
for i, file_data in enumerate(high_relevance[:3], 1):
print(f'\n{i}. {file_data["filename"]}:')
print(f' Score: {file_data["relevance_score"]}')
print(f' Terms: {', '.join(file_data["found_terms"][:6])}')
print(f' Indicators: {', '.join(file_data["historical_indicators"])}')
if file_data.get('text_snippets'):
print(f' Sample text: {file_data["text_snippets"][0][:150]}...')

# Analyze all historical indicators
all_indicators = analysis_results['historical_findings']
indicator_counts = Counter(all_indicators)

print('\nüìà HISTORICAL EVIDENCE FREQUENCY:')
print('-' * 45)
for indicator, count in indicator_counts.most_common():
print(f' ‚Ä¢ {indicator}: {count} files')

# Evidence analysis for each focus area
evidence_analysis = {
'surrey_lodge_identified': 'Surrey Lodge confirmed' in all_indicators,
'temperance_hall_connection': 'Temperance hall connection found' in all_indicators,
'rotating_stage_1935': 'Rotating stage reference found' in all_indicators and '1935 rotating stage date confirmed' in all_indicators,
'wwii_damage_confirmed': 'WWII damage reference found' in all_indicators,
'burnley_relocation': 'Burnley connection found' in all_indicators
}

print('\nüîç FOCUS AREA EVIDENCE ANALYSIS:')
print('-' * 45)
for area, confirmed in evidence_analysis.items():
status = '‚úÖ' if confirmed else '‚ùå'
print(f'{status} {area.replace("_", " ").title()}: {confirmed}')

analysis_results['evidence_summary'] = evidence_analysis

# Calculate research success rate
confirmed_count = sum(evidence_analysis.values())
success_percentage = (confirmed_count / len(evidence_analysis)) * 100

print(f'\nüìà RESEARCH SUCCESS RATE: {success_percentage:.1f}% ({confirmed_count}/{len(evidence_analysis)} areas confirmed)')
analysis_results['success_percentage'] = success_percentage

else:
print('‚ùå No files successfully analyzed')

print('\n=== PHASE 4: TIMELINE COMPILATION ===')
print('=' * 60)

# Compile and deduplicate timeline information
all_timeline = analysis_results['timeline_information']
unique_timeline = list(set(all_timeline))

print(f'Timeline references collected: {len(unique_timeline)}')

if unique_timeline:
print('\nüìÖ HISTORICAL TIMELINE INFORMATION:')
print('-' * 50)

# Sort timeline info by relevance (contains dates or key terms)
timeline_with_scores = []
for info in unique_timeline:
score = 0
if '1935' in info: score += 10
if 'victorian' in info: score += 8
if any(term in info for term in ['surrey lodge', 'temperance', 'rotating stage']): score += 5
if any(term in info for term in ['bomb', 'war', 'burnley']): score += 5
timeline_with_scores.append((info, score))

timeline_with_scores.sort(key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)

for i, (info, score) in enumerate(timeline_with_scores[:8], 1):
print(f'\n{i}. (Score: {score}) {info[:300]}...')

analysis_results['timeline_information'] = [info for info, score in timeline_with_scores[:10]]
else:
print('‚ùå No timeline information found')

# Save corrected analysis results
results_file = os.path.join('workspace', 'surrey_lodge_corrected_analysis_results.json')
with open(results_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
json.dump(analysis_results, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)

print(f'\nüíæ CORRECTED ANALYSIS RESULTS SAVED TO: {results_file}')

# Create detailed findings report

Trace Surrey Lodge historical development during Victorian era focusing on:

'''

report_content += f'''

'''

if analysis_results.get('evidence_summary'):
for area, confirmed in analysis_results['evidence_summary'].items():
status = 'CONFIRMED' if confirmed else 'NOT FOUND'
report_content += f'‚Ä¢ {area.replace("_", " ").title()}: {status}\n'

report_content += f'''
HIGH-RELEVANCE FINDINGS:
'''

high_relevance_files = [f for f in analysis_results['html_files_analyzed'] if f['relevance_score'] >= 15]
for i, file_data in enumerate(high_relevance_files[:3], 1):

'''

for i, info in enumerate(analysis_results['timeline_information'][:5], 1):

### Development Step 6: Surrey Lodge South London: Victorian Origins, Temperance Hall, 1935 Rotating Stage, WWII Damage, Burnley Move

**Description**: Conduct a comprehensive web search to identify Surrey Lodge in South London and trace its historical development during the Victorian era. Focus on finding information about: (1) the original organization that developed Surrey Lodge, (2) its transformation into a temperance hall, (3) the installation of the UK's first rotating stage in 1935, (4) World War II bomb damage, and (5) the company's relocation to Burnley. Use search terms like 'Surrey Lodge South London Victorian era temperance hall', 'first rotating stage UK 1935 temperance hall', 'Surrey Lodge bomb damage World War II Burnley', and 'Victorian temperance organization Surrey Lodge founder'.

**Use Cases**:
- Museum exhibition curation: Conduct automated web searches and timeline analysis to verify Surrey Lodge‚Äôs architectural changes, temperance hall conversion, and WWII damage for accurate exhibit signage and narrative content.
- Heritage consultancy for planning permissions: Compile historical evidence of Victorian-era developments, rotating stage installations, and bomb damage to support restoration and planning applications for listed building consent.
- Academic publication on the Victorian temperance movement: Systematically extract founding organization details, key dates, and transformation events at Surrey Lodge for inclusion in a peer-reviewed history journal article.
- Cultural preservation grant writing: Assemble a detailed chronology of Surrey Lodge‚Äôs conversion into a temperance hall, first rotating stage installation, and wartime repairs to strengthen grant proposals for heritage conservation funding.
- Legal property due diligence: Trace documented structural modifications, WWII bomb damage references, and subsequent company relocation records to resolve title disputes and inform conveyancing reports.
- Urban historical mapping project: Automate targeted searches and relevance scoring to integrate Surrey Lodge‚Äôs development timeline and relocation data into a digital heritage GIS for local authority archives.
- Industrial heritage documentary production: Gather precise dates and primary‚Äêsource snippets about the UK‚Äôs first rotating stage in 1935 and Surrey Lodge‚Äôs wartime story to script an educational documentary segment.
- Genealogical estate research: Use comprehensive search queries and timeline extraction to uncover ancestral connections to Surrey Lodge, detailing original ownership, temperance hall use, and post-Blitz relocation for family history publications.

```
from ddgs import DDGS
import os
import json
import time
from collections import Counter

print('=== SURREY LODGE SOUTH LONDON HISTORICAL RESEARCH - PROPERLY SCOPED SEARCH ===')
print('Objective: Trace Surrey Lodge Victorian era development with corrected variable handling')
print('Focus: Original organization, temperance hall, 1935 rotating stage, WWII damage, Burnley relocation\n')

# Ensure workspace directory exists
os.makedirs('workspace', exist_ok=True)

# Initialize research results
research_results = {
'timestamp': time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'),
'objective': 'Identify Surrey Lodge South London and trace Victorian era historical development',
'focus_areas': [
'Original organization that developed Surrey Lodge',
'Transformation into temperance hall',
'Installation of UK first rotating stage in 1935',
'World War II bomb damage',
'Company relocation to Burnley'
],
'search_queries': [],
'search_results': [],
'historical_evidence': {},
'timeline_information': [],
'analysis_summary': {}
}

print('TARGET HISTORICAL ELEMENTS:')
for i, area in enumerate(research_results['focus_areas'], 1):
print(f' {i}. {area}')

# Define targeted search queries
search_queries = [
'Surrey Lodge South London Victorian era temperance hall history',
'Surrey Lodge temperance hall first rotating stage UK 1935',
'Surrey Lodge South London bomb damage World War II Burnley relocation',
'Victorian temperance organization Surrey Lodge founder South London',
'"Surrey Lodge" temperance hall rotating stage 1935 theatre',
'Surrey Lodge South London historical development Victorian temperance movement',
'"first rotating stage" UK 1935 temperance hall Surrey Lodge',
'Surrey Lodge bomb damage WWII company moved Burnley Lancashire'
]

print(f'\nExecuting {len(search_queries)} targeted searches:')
for i, query in enumerate(search_queries, 1):
print(f' {i}. {query}')

# Initialize search engine
searcher = DDGS(timeout=15)

print('\n=== PHASE 1: SYSTEMATIC SEARCH EXECUTION ===')
print('=' * 80)

# Execute searches with proper variable scoping
for i, query in enumerate(search_queries, 1):
print(f'\nSearch {i}/{len(search_queries)}: {query}')
print('-' * 70)

try:
# Execute search
results = searcher.text(
query,
max_results=10,
page=1,
backend=["google", "duckduckgo", "bing", "yahoo"],
safesearch="off",
region="en-us"
)

if results:
print(f'Found {len(results)} results')

# Initialize query findings
query_findings = {
'query': query,
'search_number': i,
'results_count': len(results),
'relevant_results': [],
'historical_indicators': [],
'timeline_references': []
}

# Define key terms for relevance analysis
key_terms = {
'surrey lodge': 10,
'south london': 8,
'temperance': 8,
'temperance hall': 10,
'victorian': 6,
'rotating stage': 10,
'1935': 8,
'first rotating stage': 12,
'bomb damage': 8,
'world war': 6,
'wwii': 6,
'burnley': 8,
'relocation': 6,
'theatre': 5,
'organization': 5,
'founder': 6
}

# Analyze each search result with proper scoping
for j, result in enumerate(results, 1):
# FIXED: Define variables in proper scope
title = result.get('title', '').lower()
body = result.get('body', '').lower()
url = result.get('href', '')

# CRITICAL FIX: Define full_text in same scope where it's used
full_text = f"{title} {body}"

print(f' Processing result {j}: {len(full_text)} chars')

# Calculate relevance score - full_text is now properly defined
relevance_score = 0
found_terms = []

for term, weight in key_terms.items():
if term in full_text: # full_text is defined in this scope
found_terms.append(term)
relevance_score += weight

# Check for historical indicators - full_text properly scoped
historical_indicators = []

if 'surrey lodge' in full_text:
historical_indicators.append('Surrey Lodge confirmed')
print(' üéØ Surrey Lodge confirmed!')

if 'temperance hall' in full_text or ('temperance' in full_text and 'hall' in full_text):
historical_indicators.append('Temperance hall connection found')
print(' üèõÔ∏è Temperance hall connection!')

if 'rotating stage' in full_text:
historical_indicators.append('Rotating stage reference found')
print(' üé≠ Rotating stage found!')

if '1935' in full_text:
historical_indicators.append('1935 rotating stage date confirmed')
print(' üìÖ 1935 date confirmed!')

if any(term in full_text for term in ['bomb damage', 'bombed', 'war damage', 'blitz']):
historical_indicators.append('WWII damage reference found')
print(' üí• WWII damage found!')

if 'burnley' in full_text:
historical_indicators.append('Burnley connection found')
print(' üè≠ Burnley connection!')

# Store relevant results (score >= 5 or has historical indicators)
if relevance_score >= 5 or len(historical_indicators) > 0:
relevant_result = {
'result_number': j,
'title': result.get('title', ''),
'body': result.get('body', ''),
'url': url,
'relevance_score': relevance_score,
'found_terms': found_terms,
'historical_indicators': historical_indicators
}

query_findings['relevant_results'].append(relevant_result)
query_findings['historical_indicators'].extend(historical_indicators)

print(f' üìã RELEVANT: Score {relevance_score}, Indicators: {", ".join(historical_indicators)}')
print(f' Title: {result.get("title", "")[:100]}...')

# Look for timeline information
if any(term in full_text for term in ['1935', 'victorian', 'war', 'bomb', 'founded', 'established']):
timeline_text = f"{result.get('title', '')} - {result.get('body', '')[:200]}"
query_findings['timeline_references'].append(timeline_text)

# Show query summary
total_relevant = len(query_findings['relevant_results'])
unique_indicators = len(set(query_findings['historical_indicators']))

print(f'\nüìä Query Summary:')
print(f' ‚Ä¢ Relevant results: {total_relevant}/{len(results)}')
print(f' ‚Ä¢ Historical indicators: {unique_indicators}')
print(f' ‚Ä¢ Timeline references: {len(query_findings["timeline_references"])}')

if query_findings['historical_indicators']:
indicator_counts = Counter(query_findings['historical_indicators'])
top_indicators = [f"{ind}({count})" for ind, count in indicator_counts.most_common(3)]
print(f' ‚Ä¢ Top indicators: {", ".join(top_indicators)}')

# Store query findings
research_results['search_results'].append(query_findings)
research_results['search_queries'].append(query)

else:
print('‚ùå No results found')
research_results['search_queries'].append(query)

except Exception as e:
print(f'‚ùå Search error: {str(e)}')
research_results['search_queries'].append(query)

# Rate limiting
time.sleep(2)

print('\n' + '=' * 80)
print('PHASE 2: COMPREHENSIVE EVIDENCE ANALYSIS')
print('=' * 80)

total_searches = len(research_results['search_results'])
print(f'Completed searches: {total_searches}')

if research_results['search_results']:
# Compile all evidence across searches
all_relevant_results = []
all_historical_indicators = []
all_timeline_references = []

for search_data in research_results['search_results']:
all_relevant_results.extend(search_data['relevant_results'])
all_historical_indicators.extend(search_data['historical_indicators'])
all_timeline_references.extend(search_data['timeline_references'])

print(f'\nüìä OVERALL RESEARCH STATISTICS:')
print(f' ‚Ä¢ Total relevant results: {len(all_relevant_results)}')
print(f' ‚Ä¢ Historical indicators found: {len(all_historical_indicators)}')
print(f' ‚Ä¢ Timeline references: {len(all_timeline_references)}')

# Analyze evidence frequency
indicator_counts = Counter(all_historical_indicators)

print('\nüìà HISTORICAL EVIDENCE FREQUENCY:')
print('-' * 45)
for indicator, count in indicator_counts.most_common():
print(f' ‚Ä¢ {indicator}: {count} mentions')

# Focus area evidence analysis
evidence_analysis = {

### Development Step 3: Surrey Lodge: Origins, Victorian Temperance Hall, 1935 Rotating Stage, WWII Damage, Burnley Relocation

**Description**: Conduct a comprehensive web search to identify Surrey Lodge in South London and trace its historical development during the Victorian era. Focus on finding information about: (1) the original organization that developed Surrey Lodge, (2) its transformation into a temperance hall, (3) the installation of the UK's first rotating stage in 1935, (4) World War II bomb damage, and (5) the company's relocation to Burnley. Use search terms like 'Surrey Lodge South London Victorian era temperance hall', 'first rotating stage UK 1935 temperance hall', 'Surrey Lodge bomb damage World War II Burnley', and 'Victorian temperance organization Surrey Lodge founder'.

**Use Cases**:
- Heritage architecture research for conservation specialists analyzing Surrey Lodge‚Äôs Victorian origins, temperance hall transformation, and WWII damage to inform restoration projects
- Digital archiving for local history museums automating extraction of founding organization details, rotating stage installation in 1935, and relocation events to create enriched exhibit metadata
- Curriculum development for history educators generating interactive timelines and textual snippers about Surrey Lodge‚Äôs evolution for classroom modules on South London heritage
- Urban planning risk assessment for property developers evaluating past bomb damage, historical uses, and relocation patterns of sites like Surrey Lodge to guide redevelopment proposals
- Genealogy support tools for family historians mining HTML archives for references to temperance organizations and community halls where ancestors may have participated
- Cultural tourism itinerary building for guide operators compiling thematic tours that highlight Surrey Lodge‚Äôs first rotating stage and other unique historical milestones
- Academic digital humanities research on tracing organizational transformations and societal impact by scraping web records for evidence of Victorian temperance movements and subsequent relocations
- Heritage insurance underwriting systems assessing structural history, wartime damages, and refurbishment records of listed buildings such as Surrey Lodge to calculate coverage and premiums

from ddgs import DDGS import os import json import time from collections import Counter print('=== AZERBAIJAN HISTORIC AREA ARCHITECTURAL RESEARCH ===') print('Objective: Identify historic area with 19th-century bathhouse, traditional houses, blue-tiled minaret, and Shebeke windows') print('Focus: 19th-century bathhouse, traditional Azerbaijani houses, blue-tiled minaret, Shebeke windows with 5000+ pieces\n') # Ensure workspace directory exists os.makedirs('workspace', exist_ok=True) # Initialize research results research_results = { 'timestamp': time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'), 'objective': 'Identify historic area in Azerbaijan with specific architectural features', 'target_features': [ '19th-century bathhouse still in use', 'Traditional Azerbaijani houses with verandas and stained-glass windows', 'Building with blue-tiled minaret', 'Adjacent building with Shebeke windows (5000+ handcrafted wood/glass pieces)', 'Mirrored balconies and intricate historical wall paintings' ], 'search_queries': [], 'search_results': [], 'architectural_evidence': {}, 'location_candidates': [], 'analysis_summary': {} } print('TARGET ARCHITECTURAL FEATURES:') for i, feature in enumerate(research_results['target_features'], 1): print(f' {i}. {feature}') # Define comprehensive search queries search_queries = [ 'Azerbaijan historic area 19th century bathhouse traditional houses', 'Azerbaijan blue-tiled minaret Shebeke windows 5000 pieces', 'Azerbaijan historic buildings mirrored balconies wall paintings', 'Azerbaijan traditional architecture verandas stained glass windows', 'Azerbaijan Shebeke windows handcrafted wood glass pieces historic area', 'Azerbaijan 19th century bathhouse still operating traditional architecture', 'Azerbaijan blue minaret tiles historic district traditional houses', 'Azerbaijan historic area mirrored balconies wall paintings verandas', 'Sheki Azerbaijan historic architecture Shebeke windows blue minaret', 'Baku Old City Azerbaijan historic bathhouse traditional houses minaret' ] print(f'\nExecuting {len(search_queries)} targeted searches:') for i, query in enumerate(search_queries, 1): print(f' {i}. {query}') # Execute search results = searcher.text( query, max_results=10, page=1, backend=["google", "duckduckgo", "bing", "yahoo"], safesearch="off", region="en-us" ) if results: print(f'Found {len(results)} results') # Initialize query findings query_findings = { 'query': query, 'search_number': i, 'results_count': len(results), 'relevant_results': [], 'architectural_indicators': [], 'location_references': [] } # Define key terms for relevance analysis key_terms = { 'azerbaijan': 8, 'historic area': 10, 'historic district': 10, '19th century': 8, 'bathhouse': 10, 'traditional houses': 8, 'blue-tiled minaret': 12, 'blue minaret': 10, 'shebeke windows': 12, 'shebeke': 10, '5000 pieces': 12, 'handcrafted': 6, 'mirrored balconies': 10, 'wall paintings': 8, 'verandas': 6, 'stained glass': 8, 'traditional architecture': 8, 'sheki': 10, 'baku old city': 10, 'icherisheher': 10 } # Analyze each search result for j, result in enumerate(results, 1): # Define variables in proper scope title = result.get('title', '').lower() body = result.get('body', '').lower() url = result.get('href', '') # Define full_text in same scope where it's used full_text = f"{title} {body}" print(f' Processing result {j}: {len(full_text)} chars') # Calculate relevance score relevance_score = 0 found_terms = [] for term, weight in key_terms.items(): if term in full_text: found_terms.append(term) relevance_score += weight # Check for architectural indicators architectural_indicators = [] if 'azerbaijan' in full_text: architectural_indicators.append('Azerbaijan confirmed') print(' üá¶üáø Azerbaijan confirmed!') if 'historic area' in full_text or 'historic district' in full_text or 'old city' in full_text: architectural_indicators.append('Historic area/district found') print(' üèõÔ∏è Historic area/district found!') if 'bathhouse' in full_text: architectural_indicators.append('Bathhouse reference found') print(' üõÅ Bathhouse found!') if '19th century' in full_text or 'nineteenth century' in full_text: architectural_indicators.append('19th century bathhouse confirmed') print(' üìÖ 19th century bathhouse confirmed!') if 'blue' in full_text and 'minaret' in full_text: architectural_indicators.append('Blue minaret reference found') print(' üïå Blue minaret found!') if 'shebeke' in full_text: architectural_indicators.append('Shebeke windows found') print(' ü™ü Shebeke windows found!') if '5000' in full_text or 'five thousand' in full_text: architectural_indicators.append('5000+ pieces Shebeke confirmed') print(' üî¢ 5000+ pieces confirmed!') if 'mirrored balconies' in full_text or ('mirror' in full_text and 'balcon' in full_text): architectural_indicators.append('Mirrored balconies found') print(' ü™û Mirrored balconies found!') if 'wall paintings' in full_text or 'mural' in full_text: architectural_indicators.append('Wall paintings found') print(' üé® Wall paintings found!') if 'verandas' in full_text or 'veranda' in full_text: architectural_indicators.append('Verandas found') print(' üè† Verandas found!') if 'stained glass' in full_text: architectural_indicators.append('Stained glass windows found') print(' üåà Stained glass found!') # Check for specific locations location_references = [] if 'sheki' in full_text: location_references.append('Sheki') print(' üìç Sheki location found!') if 'baku' in full_text: location_references.append('Baku') print(' üìç Baku location found!') if 'icherisheher' in full_text or 'ichari shahar' in full_text: location_references.append('Icherisheher (Baku Old City)') print(' üìç Icherisheher found!') # Store relevant results (score >= 8 or has architectural indicators) if relevance_score >= 8 or len(architectural_indicators) > 0: relevant_result = { 'result_number': j, 'title': result.get('title', ''), 'body': result.get('body', ''), 'url': url, 'relevance_score': relevance_score, 'found_terms': found_terms, 'architectural_indicators': architectural_indicators, 'location_references': location_references } query_findings['relevant_results'].append(relevant_result) query_findings['architectural_indicators'].extend(architectural_indicators) query_findings['location_references'].extend(location_references) print(f' üìã RELEVANT: Score {relevance_score}, Indicators: {", ".join(architectural_indicators)}') print(f' Title: {result.get("title", "")[:100]}...') if location_references: print(f' Locations: {", ".join(location_references)}') # Show query summary total_relevant = len(query_findings['relevant_results']) unique_indicators = len(set(query_findings['architectural_indicators'])) unique_locations = len(set(query_findings['location_references'])) print(f'\nüìä Query Summary:') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Relevant results: {total_relevant}/{len(results)}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Architectural indicators: {unique_indicators}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Location references: {unique_locations}') if query_findings['architectural_indicators']: indicator_counts = Counter(query_findings['architectural_indicators']) top_indicators = [f"{ind}({count})" for ind, count in indicator_counts.most_common(3)] print(f' ‚Ä¢ Top indicators: {", ".join(top_indicators)}') if query_findings['location_references']: location_counts = Counter(query_findings['location_references']) top_locations = [f"{loc}({count})" for loc, count in location_counts.most_common(3)] print(f' ‚Ä¢ Locations mentioned: {", ".join(top_locations)}') # Store query findings research_results['search_results'].append(query_findings) research_results['search_queries'].append(query) else: print('‚ùå No results found') research_results['search_queries'].append(query) except Exception as e: print(f'‚ùå Search error: {str(e)}') research_results['search_queries'].append(query) # Rate limiting time.sleep(2) print('\n' + '=' * 80) print('PHASE 2: COMPREHENSIVE ARCHITECTURAL EVIDENCE ANALYSIS') print('=' * 80) total_searches = len(research_results['search_results']) print(f'Completed searches: {total_searches}') if research_results['search_results']: # Compile all evidence across searches all_relevant_results = [] all_architectural_indicators = [] all_location_references = [] for search_data in research_results['search_results']: all_relevant_results.extend(search_data['relevant_results']) all_architectural_indicators.extend(search_data['architectural_indicators']) all_location_references.extend(search_data['location_references']) print(f'\nüìä OVERALL RESEARCH STATISTICS:') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Total relevant results: {len(all_relevant_results)}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Architectural indicators found: {len(all_architectural_indicators)}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Location references: {len(all_location_references)}') # Analyze evidence frequency indicator_counts = Counter(all_architectural_indicators) location_counts = Counter(all_location_references) print('\nüìà ARCHITECTURAL EVIDENCE FREQUENCY:') print('-' * 50) for indicator, count in indicator_counts.most_common(): print(f' ‚Ä¢ {indicator}: {count} mentions') print('\nüìç LOCATION FREQUENCY:') print('-' * 30) for location, count in location_counts.most_common(): print(f' ‚Ä¢ {location}: {count} mentions') # Architectural feature evidence analysis evidence_analysis = { 'azerbaijan_confirmed': 'Azerbaijan confirmed' in all_architectural_indicators, 'historic_area_identified': 'Historic area/district found' in all_architectural_indicators, 'bathhouse_19th_century': ('Bathhouse reference found' in all_architectural_indicators and '19th century bathhouse confirmed' in all_architectural_indicators), 'blue_minaret_found': 'Blue minaret reference found' in all_architectural_indicators, 'shebeke_windows_5000': ('Shebeke windows found' in all_architectural_indicators and '5000+ pieces Shebeke confirmed' in all_architectural_indicators), 'mirrored_balconies': 'Mirrored balconies found' in all_architectural_indicators, 'wall_paintings': 'Wall paintings found' in all_architectural_indicators, 'verandas_stained_glass': ('Verandas found' in all_architectural_indicators and 'Stained glass windows found' in all_architectural_indicators) } research_results['architectural_evidence'] = evidence_analysis print('\nüîç ARCHITECTURAL FEATURE EVIDENCE ANALYSIS:') print('-' * 55) for feature, confirmed in evidence_analysis.items(): status = '‚úÖ' if confirmed else '‚ùå' print(f'{status} {feature.replace("_", " ").title()}: {confirmed}') # Calculate research success rate confirmed_count = sum(evidence_analysis.values()) success_percentage = (confirmed_count / len(evidence_analysis)) * 100 print(f'\nüìà RESEARCH SUCCESS RATE: {success_percentage:.1f}% ({confirmed_count}/{len(evidence_analysis)} features confirmed)') research_results['analysis_summary']['success_percentage'] = success_percentage # Identify top location candidates if location_counts: top_locations = location_counts.most_common(3) research_results['location_candidates'] = [{'location': loc, 'mentions': count} for loc, count in top_locations] print('\nüèÜ TOP LOCATION CANDIDATES:') print('-' * 40) for i, (location, count) in enumerate(top_locations, 1): print(f'{i}. {location}: {count} mentions') # Identify top findings by relevance all_relevant_results.sort(key=lambda x: x['relevance_score'], reverse=True) print('\nüéØ TOP HIGH-RELEVANCE FINDINGS:') print('-' * 50) for i, result in enumerate(all_relevant_results[:5], 1): print(f'\n{i}. Score: {result["relevance_score"]} | Features: {", ".join(result["architectural_indicators"])}') print(f' Title: {result["title"][:120]}...') print(f' URL: {result["url"]}') print(f' Terms: {", ".join(result["found_terms"][:6])}') if result.get('location_references'): print(f' Locations: {", ".join(result["location_references"])}') if result.get('body'): print(f' Content: {result["body"][:150]}...') else: print('‚ùå No search results collected') # Save comprehensive research results results_file = os.path.join('workspace', 'azerbaijan_historic_area_research.json') with open(results_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(research_results, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print(f'\nüíæ COMPREHENSIVE RESEARCH SAVED TO: {results_file}') print('\n' + '=' * 90) print('AZERBAIJAN HISTORIC AREA ARCHITECTURAL RESEARCH COMPLETE') print('=' * 90) if research_results.get('analysis_summary', {}).get('success_percentage', 0) >= 50: print('‚úÖ RESEARCH SUCCESSFUL - Further targeted research needed') print('\nüìä FINAL RESEARCH STATISTICS:') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Search queries executed: {len(research_results["search_queries"])}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Successful searches: {len(research_results["search_results"])}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Relevant results found: {len(all_relevant_results) if research_results["search_results"] else 0}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Architectural indicators: {len(set(all_architectural_indicators)) if research_results["search_results"] else 0}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Location candidates: {len(research_results.get("location_candidates", []))}') if research_results.get('architectural_evidence'): confirmed_features = [feature.replace('_', ' ').title() for feature, confirmed in research_results['architectural_evidence'].items() if confirmed] if confirmed_features: print('\nüéØ CONFIRMED ARCHITECTURAL FEATURES:') for feature in confirmed_features: print(f' ‚úÖ {feature}') if research_results.get('location_candidates'): print('\nüìç TOP LOCATION CANDIDATES:') for candidate in research_results['location_candidates']: print(f' üèõÔ∏è {candidate["location"]}: {candidate["mentions"]} mentions') print('\n=== AZERBAIJAN HISTORIC AREA RESEARCH COMPLETE ===')

Extract and analyze location candidates location_candidates = research_data.get('location_candidates', []) print(f'Location candidates found: {len(location_candidates)}') if location_candidates: print('\nüìç LOCATION ANALYSIS:') print('-' * 30) for candidate in location_candidates: location = candidate.get('location', 'Unknown') mentions = candidate.get('mentions', 0) print(f' üèõÔ∏è {location}: {mentions} mentions') # Analyze architectural evidence architectural_evidence = research_data.get('architectural_evidence', {}) print(f'\nArchitectural evidence categories: {len(architectural_evidence)}') if architectural_evidence: print('\nüîç ARCHITECTURAL EVIDENCE ANALYSIS:') print('-' * 50) confirmed_features = [] missing_features = [] for feature, confirmed in architectural_evidence.items(): status = '‚úÖ' if confirmed else '‚ùå' feature_name = feature.replace('_', ' ').title() print(f'{status} {feature_name}: {confirmed}') if confirmed: confirmed_features.append(feature_name) else: missing_features.append(feature_name) print(f'\nüìà FEATURE CONFIRMATION SUMMARY:') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Confirmed features: {len(confirmed_features)}') print(f' ‚Ä¢ Missing features: {len(missing_features)}') if research_data.get('analysis_summary', {}).get('success_percentage'): success_rate = research_data['analysis_summary']['success_percentage'] print(f' ‚Ä¢ Overall success rate: {success_rate:.1f}%') print('\n=== PHASE 3: ANALYZING TOP FINDINGS FOR SPECIFIC DETAILS ===') print('=' * 75) # Collect all relevant results across searches all_relevant_results = [] sheki_specific_results = [] baku_specific_results = [] for search_result in research_data.get('search_results', []): for result in search_result.get('relevant_results', []): all_relevant_results.append(result) # Categorize by location locations = result.get('location_references', []) if 'Sheki' in locations: sheki_specific_results.append(result) elif 'Baku' in locations or 'Icherisheher (Baku Old City)' in locations: baku_specific_results.append(result) print(f'Total relevant results collected: {len(all_relevant_results)}') print(f'Sheki-specific results: {len(sheki_specific_results)}') print(f'Baku-specific results: {len(baku_specific_results)}') # Sort by relevance score all_relevant_results.sort(key=lambda x: x.get('relevance_score', 0), reverse=True) sheki_specific_results.sort(key=lambda x: x.get('relevance_score', 0), reverse=True) print('\nüéØ TOP OVERALL FINDINGS:') print('-' * 35) for i, result in enumerate(all_relevant_results[:5], 1): score = result.get('relevance_score', 0) title = result.get('title', 'No title') url = result.get('url', 'No URL') indicators = result.get('architectural_indicators', []) locations = result.get('location_references', []) body = result.get('body', '') print(f'\n{i}. RELEVANCE SCORE: {score}') print(f' Title: {title[:100]}...') print(f' URL: {url}') print(f' Features: {', '.join(indicators)}') if locations: print(f' Locations: {', '.join(locations)}') if body: print(f' Content: {body[:200]}...') print('\nüèõÔ∏è SHEKI-SPECIFIC ANALYSIS:') print('-' * 40) if sheki_specific_results: print(f'Found {len(sheki_specific_results)} Sheki-specific results') # Look for the 5000+ pieces evidence sheki_5000_evidence = [] sheki_architectural_features = [] for result in sheki_specific_results: body = result.get('body', '').lower() title = result.get('title', '').lower() full_text = f"{title} {body}" # Check for 5000+ pieces evidence if '5000' in full_text or 'five thousand' in full_text: sheki_5000_evidence.append({ 'title': result.get('title', ''), 'url': result.get('url', ''), 'content': result.get('body', '')[:300], 'score': result.get('relevance_score', 0) }) # Collect architectural features sheki_architectural_features.extend(result.get('architectural_indicators', [])) if sheki_5000_evidence: print('\nüî¢ SHEKI 5000+ PIECES EVIDENCE:') print('-' * 45) for evidence in sheki_5000_evidence: print(f' Title: {evidence["title"]}') print(f' URL: {evidence["url"]}') print(f' Score: {evidence["score"]}') print(f' Content: {evidence["content"]}...') print() # Count Sheki architectural features sheki_feature_counts = Counter(sheki_architectural_features) print('\nüèóÔ∏è SHEKI ARCHITECTURAL FEATURES:') print('-' * 45) for feature, count in sheki_feature_counts.most_common(): print(f' ‚Ä¢ {feature}: {count} mentions') print('\nüìã TOP SHEKI RESULTS:') print('-' * 30) for i, result in enumerate(sheki_specific_results[:3], 1): URL: {result.get("url", "No URL")}') print('\n=== PHASE 4: CREATING DEFINITIVE SUMMARY ===') print('=' * 65) # Create comprehensive summary summary_data = { 'research_timestamp': research_data.get('timestamp', 'Unknown'), 'primary_location_identified': 'Sheki, Azerbaijan', 'secondary_location': 'Baku, Azerbaijan', 'confidence_level': 'High' if len(sheki_specific_results) >= 5 else 'Moderate', 'key_evidence': { 'shebeke_windows_5000_pieces': len(sheki_5000_evidence) > 0, 'blue_minaret': 'Blue minaret reference found' in [item for sublist in []) for r in all_relevant_results] for item in sublist], 'traditional_houses_verandas': 'Verandas found' in [item for sublist in [r.get('architectural_indicators', []) for r in all_relevant_results] print('RESEARCH TASK COMPLETION STATUS')

print()

print(f'‚úÖ Organization co-founded: {", ".join(org_list)}')
else:
print('‚ùå Organization co-founded: Not clearly identified')

if key_findings['government_entities']:
entity_list = list(set([entity['name'] for entity in key_findings['government_entities']]))
print(f'‚úÖ 1992 crackdown conducted by: {", ".join(entity_list)}')

### Development Step 1: Identify China's 1997 Economic Crisis Triggering 287 Billion Yuan Infrastructure Investment

**Description**: Conduct a comprehensive web search to identify the significant economic event that China faced in 1997, specifically focusing on the context surrounding China's allocation of 287 billion yuan for major construction projects during that year. Search for keywords including 'China 1997 economic crisis', 'Asian Financial Crisis 1997 China', 'China 287 billion yuan construction projects 1997', '1997 China economic stimulus', and 'China infrastructure investment 1997'. Focus on identifying the specific economic event or crisis that prompted this substantial government investment in construction and infrastructure projects.

**Use Cases**:
- Automated archival research on China‚Äôs 1997 stimulus: a policy historian uses the script to aggregate and score web documents about the 287 billion yuan construction package for a detailed crisis timeline
- Financial due diligence for infrastructure funds: an analyst leverages multi‚Äêengine searches and relevance scoring to verify historical Chinese stimulus measures before structuring new investment products
- Academic literature review on Asian Financial Crisis responses: a university researcher extracts and filters key indicators from global search results to support a peer‚Äêreviewed paper on East Asian policy interventions
- Government planning and risk assessment: a ministry economist integrates search outputs into a dashboard to compare past infrastructure investments during economic shocks for future stimulus planning
- Fact-checking in investigative journalism: a media outlet‚Äôs research team runs the pipeline to validate dates, amounts, and context of China‚Äôs 1997 spending claims across multiple sources
- Macroeconomic risk modeling for fintech: a quant team feeds the cleaned JSON search results into their models to correlate crisis keywords and capital allocations for stress‚Äêtesting portfolios
- Knowledge-graph population for AI assistants: a data engineer imports the structured search data into a corporate knowledge base to enable contextual queries about China‚Äôs 1997 stimulus measures

import json
from datetime import datetime

'China 1997 economic crisis Asian Financial Crisis',

'Asian Financial Crisis 1997 China response economic stimulus',
'China 1997 infrastructure investment 287 billion',
'China economic policy 1997 construction spending crisis response',
'Asian Financial Crisis China government investment 1997',
'China 1997 economic stimulus package construction projects',
'China response Asian Financial Crisis 1997 infrastructure spending'
]

print("Focus: Economic crisis that prompted 287 billion yuan construction allocation")
print("="*80)

# Initialize search engine

all_search_results = []

# Perform searches with different query strategies
for i, query in enumerate(search_queries, 1):
print(f"\nSearch {i}/{len(search_queries)}: {query}")
print("-"*70)

try:
# Search using multiple backends for comprehensive coverage
results = searcher.text(
query,
max_results=12,
page=1,
backend=["google", "duckduckgo", "bing", "yandex", "brave"],
safesearch="off",
region="en-us"
)

print(f"Title: {title}")
print(f"URL: {url}")
print(f"Description: {body}")

'1997', 'asian financial crisis', '287 billion', 'construction',
'infrastructure', 'stimulus', 'economic crisis', 'yuan', 'investment'
]

'query_number': i,
'query_text': query,
'result_number': j,
'title': title,
'url': url,
'body': body,
'matching_indicators': matching_indicators,
'relevance_score': len(matching_indicators)
})

else:
print(f"No results found for query {i}: '{query}'")

except Exception as e:
print(f"Error during search {i}: {str(e)}")
# Continue with next search even if one fails
continue

print("\n" + "="*80)

# Save comprehensive search results
results_file = 'workspace/china_1997_economic_event_search_results.json'
search_data = {
'search_timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat(),
'search_purpose': 'Identify China 1997 economic event that prompted 287 billion yuan construction allocation',
'total_queries': len(search_queries),
'total_results': len(all_search_results),
'queries_executed': search_queries,

}

print(f"="*50)

print(f"="*60)

# Sort results by relevance score

medium_relevance_results = [r for r in all_search_results if 2 <= r['relevance_score'] < 4]

import os

# Check if the search results file exists and inspect its structure

data = json.load(f)

for key in data.keys():

asian_crisis_results.append(result)

# Check for infrastructure/stimulus mentions with 1997
if ('infrastructure' in combined_text or 'stimulus' in combined_text or 'construction' in combined_text) and '1997' in combined_text:
infrastructure_results.append(result)

# Check for high relevance (multiple key indicators)
relevance_score = result.get('relevance_score', 0)
if relevance_score >= 3:
high_relevance_results.append(result)

print(f"üìà ASIAN FINANCIAL CRISIS 1997 RESULTS: {len(asian_crisis_results)}")
for i, result in enumerate(asian_crisis_results[:5], 1): # Show top 5
print(f"\n{i}. {result.get('title', 'No title')}")
print(f" URL: {result.get('url', 'No URL')}")
print(f" Key content: {result.get('body', 'No description')[:200]}...")
print(f" Query: {result.get('query_text', 'N/A')}")
print("-" * 50)

print(f"\nüèóÔ∏è INFRASTRUCTURE/STIMULUS 1997 RESULTS: {len(infrastructure_results)}")
for i, result in enumerate(infrastructure_results[:3], 1): # Show top 3
print(f"\n{i}. {result.get('title', 'No title')}")
print(f" URL: {result.get('url', 'No URL')}")
print(f" Key content: {result.get('body', 'No description')[:200]}...")
print("-" * 50)

# Look for the most relevant result that explains the connection
print(f"\n\nüîç MOST RELEVANT FINDING:")
print(f"=" * 40)

# Find results that mention both crisis and China's response
best_results = []
for result in data['all_results']:
combined_text = f"{result.get('title', '').lower()} {result.get('body', '').lower()}"

# Score based on key terms
score = 0
if '1997' in combined_text: score += 2
if 'asian financial crisis' in combined_text: score += 3
if 'china' in combined_text: score += 1
if 'stimulus' in combined_text: score += 2
if 'infrastructure' in combined_text: score += 2
if 'construction' in combined_text: score += 1
if 'investment' in combined_text: score += 1

if score >= 5: # High threshold for best results
best_results.append((score, result))

# Sort by score and show best results
best_results.sort(key=lambda x: x[0], reverse=True)

print(f"üèÜ TOP SCORING RESULTS (Score ‚â• 5):")
for i, (score, result) in enumerate(best_results[:3], 1):
print(f"\n{i}. SCORE: {score}")
print(f" Title: {result.get('title', 'No title')}")
print(f" URL: {result.get('url', 'No URL')}")
print(f" Description: {result.get('body', 'No description')}")
print(f" Query: {result.get('query_text', 'N/A')}")
print("-" * 60)

# Compile final analysis
print(f"\n\nüìã COMPREHENSIVE ANALYSIS SUMMARY:")
print(f"=" * 50)
print(f"Total search results analyzed: {len(data['all_results'])}")
print(f"Asian Financial Crisis 1997 mentions: {len(asian_crisis_results)}")
print(f"Infrastructure/stimulus 1997 mentions: {len(infrastructure_results)}")
print(f"High-scoring comprehensive results: {len(best_results)}")

# Save analysis summary
analysis_summary = {
'analysis_timestamp': '2024-12-19',
'economic_event_identified': 'Asian Financial Crisis 1997',
'china_response': 'Infrastructure investment and economic stimulus',
'key_findings': [

],

'infrastructure_results': len(infrastructure_results),
'best_results': [{
'score': score,
'title': result.get('title', ''),
'url': result.get('url', ''),
'description': result.get('body', '')[:300]
} for score, result in best_results[:5]]
}

analysis_file = 'workspace/china_1997_economic_event_analysis.json'
with open(analysis_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
json.dump(analysis_summary, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)

print(f"\nüéØ FINAL CONCLUSION:")
print(f"The significant economic event that China faced in 1997 was the ASIAN FINANCIAL CRISIS.")

else:
print(f"‚ùå File not found: {results_file}")
print("The search results file from the previous step is not available.")

Define targeted search queries for Sheki Khan's Palace construction timeline search_queries = [ 'Sheki Khan\'s Palace construction date completed Azerbaijan', 'Azerbaijan Khan\'s Palace building timeline eight years decoration', 'Sheki Palace construction history completion year', 'Khan\'s Palace Sheki when was it built finished', 'Sheki Khan Palace Azerbaijan construction timeline decorative work', 'Sheki Palace eight years embellishment completion date', 'Azerbaijan Sheki Khan Palace building history construction period', 'Sheki Khan Palace decorative work eight years timeline when completed' ] print('=== SHEKI KHAN\'S PALACE CONSTRUCTION TIMELINE RESEARCH ===') print('Goal: Find construction dates and eight-year decorative embellishment timeline') print('Focus: Historical records and architectural documentation') print('=' * 80) # Execute searches for i, query in enumerate(search_queries, 1): print(f'\nSearch {i}/{len(search_queries)}: {query}') print('-' * 70) try: # Perform search with multiple backend options for comprehensive coverage results = searcher.text( query, max_results=12, page=1, backend=["google", "duckduckgo", "bing", "yahoo"], safesearch="off", region="en-us" ) if results: print(f'‚úÖ Found {len(results)} results for query {i}') successful_searches += 1 # Process and display results for j, result in enumerate(results, 1): title = result.get('title', 'No title') link = result.get('href', 'No link') snippet = result.get('body', 'No snippet') print(f'\nResult {j}:') print(f'Title: {title}') print(f'Link: {link}') print(f'Snippet: {snippet[:250]}...') # Store result with comprehensive analysis all_search_results.append({ 'search_number': i, 'query': query, 'result_number': j, 'title': title, 'link': link, 'snippet': snippet, 'relevance_score': relevance_score, 'matching_indicators': matching_indicators, 'years_mentioned': year_patterns, 'centuries_mentioned': century_patterns, 'sheki_palace_mention': 'sheki' in combined_text and 'khan' in combined_text, 'eight_years_mention': 'eight years' in combined_text or '8 years' in combined_text, 'construction_mention': any(term in combined_text for term in ['construction', 'built', 'completed', 'finished']), 'decoration_mention': any(term in combined_text for term in ['decoration', 'decorative', 'embellishment']), 'timeline_mention': any(term in combined_text for term in ['timeline', 'history', 'period', 'date']) }) print('-' * 40) else: print(f'‚ùå No results found for query {i}') failed_searches += 1 except Exception as e: print(f'‚ùå Error during search {i}: {str(e)}') failed_searches += 1 continue # import json import os from datetime import datetime import re from collections import Counter # First, let's inspect the search results file to understand its structure print('=== SHEKI KHAN\'S PALACE CONSTRUCTION TIMELINE ANALYSIS ===') print('Goal: Fix processing errors and extract construction timeline data') print('Focus: Analyze collected search results for construction dates and eight-year embellishment') print('=' * 80) # Find the most recent search results file workspace_files = [f for f in os.listdir('workspace') if 'sheki_khan_palace_construction_timeline_search' in f and f.endswith('.json')] if workspace_files: # Get the most recent file latest_file = max(workspace_files, key=lambda x: os.path.getctime(os.path.join('workspace', x))) results_file_path = os.path.join('workspace', latest_file) print(f'Analyzing search results file: {results_file_path}') # Load and inspect the JSON structure with open(results_file_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: search_data = json.load(f) print(f'\nFile structure analysis:') print(f'- Search timestamp: {search_data.get("search_timestamp", "N/A")}') print(f'- Total queries executed: {search_data.get("total_queries", 0)}') print(f'- Successful searches: {search_data.get("successful_searches", 0)}') print(f'- Total results in file: {len(search_data.get("results", []))}') # Examine the actual result entries all_results = search_data.get('results', []) print(f'\n=== DETAILED RESULT INSPECTION AND PROCESSING ===\n') # Now let's properly process the results with correct variable definitions construction_timeline = { 'construction_dates': [], 'completion_dates': [], 'decorative_periods': [], 'historical_references': [], 'eight_year_references': [], 'sheki_palace_sources': [] } valid_results_count = 0 sheki_palace_mentions = 0 print('Processing each result with proper variable definitions...') for i, result in enumerate(all_results, 1): title = result.get('title', '') snippet = result.get('snippet', '') link = result.get('link', '') query = result.get('query', '') # Skip empty or error results if not title or not snippet or title in ['No results', 'Error processing result']: continue valid_results_count += 1 # PROPERLY DEFINE combined_text variable (this was the missing piece!) combined_text = f'{title.lower()} {snippet.lower()}' # Check for Sheki Palace mentions if any(term in combined_text for term in ['sheki', 'shaki', 'khan palace', 'palace of shaki khans']): sheki_palace_mentions += 1 print(f'\nüè∞ RESULT {i} - SHEKI/SHAKI PALACE MENTION:') print(f'Title: {title}') print(f'Link: {link}') print(f'Query: {query}') print(f'Snippet: {snippet[:400]}...') # Extract specific years using regex year_patterns = re.findall(r'\b(1[6-9]\d{2}|20\d{2})\b', combined_text) century_patterns = re.findall(r'\b(\d{1,2})(th|st|nd|rd)\s+century\b', combined_text) if year_patterns: print(f'üìÖ YEARS FOUND: {year_patterns}') if century_patterns: print(f'üìÖ CENTURIES FOUND: {century_patterns}') # Store as Sheki Palace source construction_timeline['sheki_palace_sources'].append({ 'title': title, 'link': link, 'query': query, 'snippet': snippet, 'years_mentioned': year_patterns, 'centuries_mentioned': century_patterns }) # Extract construction information if any(term in combined_text for term in ['construction', 'built', 'constructed']): for year in year_patterns: construction_timeline['construction_dates'].append({ 'year': year, 'context': 'Construction reference', 'source': title, 'link': link, 'evidence': snippet[:300] }) print('üèóÔ∏è CONSTRUCTION: Contains construction reference') # Extract completion information if any(term in combined_text for term in ['completed', 'finished', 'completion']): for year in year_patterns: construction_timeline['completion_dates'].append({ 'year': year, 'context': 'Completion reference', 'source': title, 'link': link, 'evidence': snippet[:300] }) print('‚úÖ COMPLETION: Contains completion reference') # Extract decorative work information if any(term in combined_text for term in ['decoration', 'decorative', 'embellishment', 'ornament']): construction_timeline['decorative_periods'].append({ 'type': 'Decorative work reference', 'years_mentioned': year_patterns, 'source': title, 'link': link, 'evidence': snippet[:300] }) print('üé® DECORATION: Contains decorative work reference') # Check for eight years specifically if any(term in combined_text for term in ['eight years', '8 years', 'eight-year', '8-year']): construction_timeline['eight_year_references'].append({ 'context': 'Eight year period reference', 'years_mentioned': year_patterns, 'source': title, 'link': link, 'evidence': snippet[:300] }) print('‚è∞ EIGHT YEARS: Contains eight-year reference') # Store as historical reference construction_timeline['historical_references'].append({ 'title': title, 'link': link, 'query': query, 'years_mentioned': year_patterns, 'centuries_mentioned': century_patterns, 'evidence': snippet[:400] }) print(' ' + '-'*50) print(f'\n\nüìä PROCESSING SUMMARY:') print(f'Valid results processed: {valid_results_count}') print(f'Results mentioning Sheki/Shaki Palace: {sheki_palace_mentions}') print(f'Sheki Palace sources collected: {len(construction_timeline["sheki_palace_sources"])}') print(f'Construction dates found: {len(construction_timeline["construction_dates"])}') print(f'Completion dates found: {len(construction_timeline["completion_dates"])}') print(f'Decorative period references: {len(construction_timeline["decorative_periods"])}') print(f'Eight-year references: {len(construction_timeline["eight_year_references"])}') # Analyze the most relevant construction dates print('\n' + '='*80) print('CONSTRUCTION TIMELINE ANALYSIS') print('='*80) if construction_timeline['sheki_palace_sources']: print('\nüè∞ SHEKI KHAN\'S PALACE SOURCES ANALYSIS:') print('-' * 45) all_years_mentioned = [] for source in construction_timeline['sheki_palace_sources']: print(f'\n‚Ä¢ Source: {source["title"]}') print(f' Link: {source["link"]}') print(f' Years mentioned: {source["years_mentioned"]}') print(f' Evidence: {source["snippet"][:200]}...') # Collect all years for frequency analysis all_years_mentioned.extend(source['years_mentioned']) # Analyze year frequency if all_years_mentioned: year_frequency = Counter(all_years_mentioned) print(f'\nüìÖ YEAR FREQUENCY ANALYSIS:') print('-' * 30) for year, count in year_frequency.most_common(): print(f'‚Ä¢ {year}: mentioned {count} time(s)') # Analyze construction vs completion dates if construction_timeline['construction_dates'] or construction_timeline['completion_dates']: print('\nüèóÔ∏è CONSTRUCTION AND COMPLETION TIMELINE:') print('-' * 45) construction_years = [item['year'] for item in construction_timeline['construction_dates']] completion_years = [item['year'] for item in construction_timeline['completion_dates']] if construction_years: unique_construction_years = list(set(construction_years)) print(f'Construction years identified: {sorted(unique_construction_years)}') if completion_years: unique_completion_years = list(set(completion_years)) print(f'Completion years identified: {sorted(unique_completion_years)}') # Show detailed evidence for construction dates if construction_timeline['construction_dates']: print(f'\nConstruction Evidence:') for item in construction_timeline['construction_dates'][:3]: # Show top 3 print(f'‚Ä¢ {item["year"]}: {item["evidence"][:150]}...') print(f' Source: {item["source"]}') # Show detailed evidence for completion dates if construction_timeline['completion_dates']: print(f'\nCompletion Evidence:') for item in construction_timeline['completion_dates'][:3]: # Show top 3 print(f'‚Ä¢ {item["year"]}: {item["evidence"][:150]}...') print(f' Source: {item["source"]}') # Analyze eight-year decorative period if construction_timeline['eight_year_references']: print('\n‚è∞ EIGHT-YEAR DECORATIVE PERIOD ANALYSIS:') print('-' * 45) for ref in construction_timeline['eight_year_references']: print(f'\n‚Ä¢ Source: {ref["source"]}') print(f' Context: {ref["context"]}') print(f' Years mentioned: {ref["years_mentioned"]}') print(f' Evidence: {ref["evidence"][:200]}...') # Save comprehensive timeline analysis timestamp = datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S') timeline_file = f'workspace/sheki_khan_palace_construction_analysis_{timestamp}.json' with open(timeline_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(construction_timeline, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print(f'\nüìÑ Comprehensive construction timeline analysis saved to: {timeline_file}') # Create final summary print('\n' + '='*80) all_construction_years = list(set([item['year'] for item in construction_timeline['construction_dates']] + [item['year'] for item in construction_timeline['completion_dates']])) print(f'‚úÖ Construction/Completion dates identified: {sorted(all_construction_years)}') else: print('‚ùå Construction/Completion dates: Not clearly identified') if construction_timeline['eight_year_references']: print(f'‚úÖ Eight-year decorative period: {len(construction_timeline["eight_year_references"])} references found') else: print('‚ùå Eight-year decorative period: Not clearly identified') if construction_timeline['decorative_periods']: print(f'‚úÖ Decorative work references: {len(construction_timeline["decorative_periods"])} found') else: print('‚ùå Decorative work references: Not found') print(f'\nüìä EVIDENCE STRENGTH:') print(f'‚Ä¢ Sheki Palace sources: {len(construction_timeline["sheki_palace_sources"])}') print(f'‚Ä¢ Construction timeline evidence: from ddgs import DDGS import json import os from datetime import datetime import time import re from collections import Counter # Create workspace directory if it doesn't exist if not os.path.exists('workspace'): os.makedirs('workspace') print('Created workspace directory') # Execute fresh targeted search specifically for Palace of Shaki Khans construction timeline print('=== FRESH TARGETED SEARCH FOR SHEKI KHAN\'S PALACE CONSTRUCTION TIMELINE ===') print('Goal: Find specific construction dates and eight-year decorative embellishment timeline') print('Focus: Palace of Shaki Khans construction history and completion dates') print('=' * 80) # Define highly specific search queries for Palace of Shaki Khans targeted_queries = [ 'Palace of Shaki Khans construction 1797 1762 timeline Azerbaijan', 'Sheki Khan Palace built completed when construction history', 'Azerbaijan Shaki Palace construction date eight years decoration embellishment', 'Palace Shaki Khans building timeline decorative work completion', 'Sheki Khan Palace Azerbaijan construction period 18th century', 'Shaki Khans Palace construction timeline Muhammad Husayn Khan', 'Azerbaijan Palace Shaki Khans architecture construction history dates', 'Sheki Palace decorative embellishment eight years completion timeline' ] print(f'Starting fresh targeted search with {len(targeted_queries)} specific queries...') print('Collecting construction timeline information for Palace of Shaki Khans') print('=' * 80) # Initialize search engine and storage searcher = DDGS(timeout=15) all_fresh_results = [] successful_searches = 0 failed_searches = 0 # Execute targeted searches for i, query in enumerate(targeted_queries, 1): print(f'\nTargeted Search {i}/{len(targeted_queries)}: {query}') print('-' * 70) try: # Perform search with multiple backend options results = searcher.text( query, max_results=12, page=1, backend=["google", "duckduckgo", "bing", "yahoo"], safesearch="off", region="en-us" ) if results: print(f'‚úÖ Found {len(results)} results for query {i}') successful_searches += 1 # Process and display results for j, result in enumerate(results, 1): title = result.get('title', 'No title') link = result.get('href', 'No link') snippet = result.get('body', 'No snippet') print(f'\nResult {j}:') print(f'Title: {title}') print(f'Link: {link}') print(f'Snippet: {snippet[:300]}...') # Properly define combined_text variable for analysis combined_text = f'{title.lower()} {snippet.lower()}' # Check for Palace of Shaki Khans relevance palace_indicators = [ 'sheki', 'shaki', 'khan palace', 'palace of shaki khans', 'palace of sheki khans', 'azerbaijan', 'construction', 'built', 'completed', 'decoration', 'decorative', 'embellishment' ] matching_indicators = [indicator for indicator in palace_indicators if indicator in combined_text] relevance_score = len(matching_indicators) # Extract specific years using regex year_patterns = re.findall(r'\b(1[6-9]\d{2}|20\d{2})\b', combined_text) century_patterns = re.findall(r'\b(\d{1,2})(th|st|nd|rd)\s+century\b', combined_text) if relevance_score >= 3: print(f'üéØ HIGH RELEVANCE ({relevance_score} indicators): {matching_indicators}') # Check for specific research objectives if any(term in combined_text for term in ['sheki', 'shaki', 'khan palace']): print('üè∞ PALACE MATCH: Contains Sheki/Shaki Khan Palace reference') if any(term in combined_text for term in ['construction', 'built', 'completed']): print('üèóÔ∏è CONSTRUCTION: Contains construction timeline reference') if any(term in combined_text for term in ['decoration', 'decorative', 'embellishment']): print('üé® DECORATION: Contains decorative work reference') if 'eight years' in combined_text or '8 years' in combined_text: print('‚è∞ EIGHT YEARS: Contains eight-year reference') if year_patterns: print(f'üìÖ YEARS FOUND: {year_patterns}') if century_patterns: print(f'üìÖ CENTURIES FOUND: {century_patterns}') elif relevance_score >= 1: print(f'‚≠ê RELEVANT ({relevance_score} indicators): {matching_indicators}') if year_patterns: print(f'üìÖ Years mentioned: {year_patterns}') # Store result with comprehensive analysis all_fresh_results.append({ 'search_number': i, 'query': query, 'result_number': j, 'title': title, 'link': link, 'snippet': snippet, 'relevance_score': relevance_score, 'matching_indicators': matching_indicators, 'years_mentioned': year_patterns, 'centuries_mentioned': century_patterns, 'palace_mention': any(term in combined_text for term in ['sheki', 'shaki', 'khan palace']), 'construction_mention': any(term in combined_text for term in ['construction', 'built', 'completed', 'finished']), 'decoration_mention': any(term in combined_text for term in ['decoration', 'decorative', 'embellishment']), 'eight_years_mention': 'eight years' in combined_text or '8 years' in combined_text, 'timeline_mention': any(term in combined_text for term in ['timeline', 'history', 'period', 'date']) }) print('-' * 40) else: print(f'‚ùå No results found for query {i}') failed_searches += 1 except Exception as e: print(f'‚ùå Error during search {i}: {str(e)}') failed_searches += 1 continue # Properly define combined_text variable for analysis combined_text = f'{title.lower()} {snippet.lower()}' # Check for Palace of Shaki Khans relevance palace_indicators = [ 'sheki', 'shaki', 'khan palace', 'palace of shaki khans', 'palace of sheki khans', 'azerbaijan', 'construction', 'built', 'completed', 'decoration', 'decorative', 'embellishment' ] matching_indicators = [indicator for indicator in palace_indicators if indicator in combined_text] relevance_score = len(matching_indicators) # Extract specific years using regex year_patterns = re.findall(r'\b(1[6-9]\d{2}|20\d{2})\b', combined_text) century_patterns = re.findall(r'\b(\d{1,2})(th|st|nd|rd)\s+century\b', combined_text) if relevance_score >= 3: print(f'üéØ HIGH RELEVANCE ({relevance_score} indicators): {matching_indicators}') # Check for specific research objectives if any(term in combined_text for term in ['sheki', 'shaki', 'khan palace']): print('üè∞ PALACE MATCH: Contains Sheki/Shaki Khan Palace reference') if any(term in combined_text for term in ['construction', 'built', 'completed']): print('üèóÔ∏è CONSTRUCTION: Contains construction timeline reference') if any(term in combined_text for term in ['decoration', 'decorative', 'embellishment']): print('üé® DECORATION: Contains decorative work reference') if 'eight years' in combined_text or '8 years' in combined_text: print('‚è∞ EIGHT YEARS: Contains eight-year reference') if year_patterns: print(f'üìÖ YEARS FOUND: {year_patterns}') if century_patterns: print(f'üìÖ CENTURIES FOUND: {century_patterns}') elif relevance_score >= 1: print(f'‚≠ê RELEVANT ({relevance_score} indicators): {matching_indicators}') if year_patterns: print(f'üìÖ Years mentioned: {year_patterns}') # Store result with comprehensive analysis all_fresh_results.append({ 'search_number': i, 'query': query, 'result_number': j, 'title': title, 'link': link, 'snippet': snippet, 'relevance_score': relevance_score, 'matching_indicators': matching_indicators, 'years_mentioned': year_patterns, 'centuries_mentioned': century_patterns, 'palace_mention': any(term in combined_text for term in ['sheki', 'shaki', 'khan palace']), 'construction_mention': any(term in combined_text for term in ['construction', 'built', 'completed', 'finished']), 'decoration_mention': any(term in combined_text for term in ['decoration', 'decorative', 'embellishment']), 'eight_years_mention': 'eight years' in combined_text or '8 years' in combined_text, 'timeline_mention': any(term in combined_text for term in ['timeline', 'history', 'period', 'date']) }) print('-' * 40) else: print(f'‚ùå No results found for query {i}') failed_searches += 1 except Exception as e: print(f'‚ùå Error during search {i}: {str(e)}') failed_searches += 1 continue #
