from ddgs import DDGS import json import os from datetime import datetime import time import re from collections import Counter # Create workspace directory if it doesn't exist if not os.path.exists('workspace'): os.makedirs('workspace') print('Created workspace directory') # Execute fresh targeted search with FIXED variable definition print('=== FIXED TARGETED SEARCH FOR SHEKI KHAN\'S PALACE CONSTRUCTION TIMELINE ===') print('Goal: Find specific construction dates and eight-year decorative embellishment timeline') print('Focus: Palace of Shaki Khans construction history with PROPER variable handling') print('=' * 80) # Define highly specific search queries for Palace of Shaki Khans targeted_queries = [ 'Palace of Shaki Khans construction 1797 1762 timeline Azerbaijan', 'Sheki Khan Palace built completed when construction history', 'Azerbaijan Shaki Palace construction date eight years decoration embellishment', 'Palace Shaki Khans building timeline decorative work completion', 'Sheki Khan Palace Azerbaijan construction period 18th century', 'Shaki Khans Palace construction timeline Muhammad Husayn Khan' ] print(f'Starting FIXED targeted search with {len(targeted_queries)} specific queries...') print('Collecting construction timeline information for Palace of Shaki Khans') print('=' * 80) # Initialize search engine and storage searcher = DDGS(timeout=15) all_fresh_results = [] successful_searches = 0 failed_searches = 0 # Execute targeted searches with FIXED processing for i, query in enumerate(targeted_queries, 1): print(f'\nTargeted Search {i}/{len(targeted_queries)}: {query}') print('-' * 70) try: # Perform search with multiple backend options results = searcher.text( query, max_results=10, page=1, backend=["google", "duckduckgo", "bing"], safesearch="off", region="en-us" ) if results: print(f'‚úÖ Found {len(results)} results for query {i}') successful_searches += 1 # Process and display results with FIXED variable handling for j, result in enumerate(results, 1): title = result.get('title', 'No title') link = result.get('href', 'No link') snippet = result.get('body', 'No snippet') print(f'\nResult {j}:') print(f'Title: {title}') print(f'Link: {link}') print(f'Snippet: {snippet[:300]}...') # CRITICAL FIX: Define combined_text BEFORE using it combined_text = f'{title.lower()} {snippet.lower()}' # Check for Palace of Shaki Khans relevance palace_indicators = [ 'sheki', 'shaki', 'khan palace', 'palace of shaki khans', 'palace of sheki khans', 'azerbaijan', 'construction', 'built', 'completed', 'decoration', 'decorative', 'embellishment' ] matching_indicators = [indicator for indicator in palace_indicators if indicator in combined_text] relevance_score = len(matching_indicators) # Extract specific years using regex year_patterns = re.findall(r'\b(1[6-9]\d{2}|20\d{2})\b', combined_text) century_patterns = re.findall(r'\b(\d{1,2})(th|st|nd|rd)\s+century\b', combined_text) if relevance_score >= 3: print(f'üéØ HIGH RELEVANCE ({relevance_score} indicators): {matching_indicators}') # Check for specific research objectives if any(term in combined_text for term in ['sheki', 'shaki', 'khan palace']): print('üè∞ PALACE MATCH: Contains Sheki/Shaki Khan Palace reference') if any(term in combined_text for term in ['construction', 'built', 'completed']): print('üèóÔ∏è CONSTRUCTION: Contains construction timeline reference') if any(term in combined_text for term in ['decoration', 'decorative', 'embellishment']): print('üé® DECORATION: Contains decorative work reference') if 'eight years' in combined_text or '8 years' in combined_text: print('‚è∞ EIGHT YEARS: Contains eight-year reference') if year_patterns: print(f'üìÖ YEARS FOUND: {year_patterns}') if century_patterns: print(f'üìÖ CENTURIES FOUND: {century_patterns}') elif relevance_score >= 1: print(f'‚≠ê RELEVANT ({relevance_score} indicators): {matching_indicators}') if year_patterns: print(f'üìÖ Years mentioned: {year_patterns}') # Store result with comprehensive analysis all_fresh_results.append({ 'search_number': i, 'query': query, 'result_number': j, 'title': title, 'link': link, 'snippet': snippet, 'relevance_score': relevance_score, 'matching_indicators': matching_indicators, 'years_mentioned': year_patterns, 'centuries_mentioned': century_patterns, 'palace_mention': any(term in combined_text for term in ['sheki', 'shaki', 'khan palace']), 'construction_mention': any(term in combined_text for term in ['construction', 'built', 'completed', 'finished']), 'decoration_mention': any(term in combined_text for term in ['decoration', 'decorative', 'embellishment']), 'eight_years_mention': 'eight years' in combined_text or '8 years' in combined_text, 'timeline_mention': any(term in combined_text for term in ['timeline', 'history', 'period', 'date']) }) print('-' * 40) else: print(f'‚ùå No results found for query {i}') failed_searches += 1 except Exception as e: print(f'‚ùå Error during search {i}: {str(e)}') failed_searches += 1 continue # Small delay between searches to avoid rate limiting time.sleep(1) print('\n' + '=' * 80) # Save comprehensive fresh search results timestamp = datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S') fresh_results_file = f'workspace/sheki_palace_FIXED_targeted_search_{timestamp}.json' search_data = { 'search_timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat(), 'search_purpose': 'FIXED targeted search for Palace of Shaki Khans construction timeline', 'research_objectives': [ 'Identify construction start date', 'Find completion date after eight-year decorative embellishment', 'Extract specific timeline for decorative work', 'Locate historical construction records for Palace of Shaki Khans' ], 'total_queries': len(targeted_queries), 'successful_searches': successful_searches, 'failed_searches': failed_searches, 'total_results': len(all_fresh_results), 'queries_executed': targeted_queries, 'results': all_fresh_results } with open(fresh_results_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(search_data, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print(f'\n\nüìä FIXED SEARCH EXECUTION SUMMARY:') print(f'Total queries executed: {len(targeted_queries)}') print(f'Successful searches: {successful_searches}') print(f'Failed searches: {failed_searches}') print(f'Total results collected: {len(all_fresh_results)}') print(f'Fixed search results saved to: {fresh_results_file}') # Immediate analysis of SUCCESSFULLY collected results print('\n\nüîç ANALYSIS OF SUCCESSFULLY COLLECTED CONSTRUCTION TIMELINE DATA:') print('=' * 75) # Filter results by relevance and specific content high_relevance_results = [r for r in all_fresh_results if r['relevance_score'] >= 4] palace_mentions = [r for r in all_fresh_results if r['palace_mention']] construction_mentions = [r for r in all_fresh_results if r['construction_mention']] decoration_mentions = [r for r in all_fresh_results if r['decoration_mention']] eight_years_mentions = [r for r in all_fresh_results if r['eight_years_mention']] results_with_years = [r for r in all_fresh_results if r['years_mentioned']] print(f'\nüìã FIXED RESULT CATEGORIZATION:') print(f'High relevance results (4+ indicators): {len(high_relevance_results)}') print(f'Results mentioning Palace/Sheki/Shaki: {len(palace_mentions)}') print(f'Results with construction references: {len(construction_mentions)}') print(f'Results with decoration references: {len(decoration_mentions)}') print(f'Results mentioning eight years: {len(eight_years_mentions)}') print(f'Results containing specific years: {len(results_with_years)}') # Extract and analyze construction timeline information print('\n\nüèóÔ∏è CONSTRUCTION TIMELINE EXTRACTION FROM COLLECTED DATA:') print('=' * 60) construction_timeline = { 'construction_dates': [], 'completion_dates': [], 'decorative_periods': [], 'eight_year_references': [], 'palace_sources': [], 'year_frequency': {} } # Collect all years mentioned across palace-related results all_years_mentioned = [] for result in palace_mentions: all_years_mentioned.extend(result['years_mentioned']) if all_years_mentioned: year_frequency = Counter(all_years_mentioned) construction_timeline['year_frequency'] = dict(year_frequency) print(f'üìÖ CONSTRUCTION YEAR FREQUENCY ANALYSIS:') print('-' * 40) for year, count in year_frequency.most_common(): print(f'‚Ä¢ {year}: mentioned {count} time(s)') # Analyze palace results for specific timeline information for result in palace_mentions: title = result['title'] snippet = result['snippet'] link = result['link'] years = result['years_mentioned'] print(f'\nüè∞ Analyzing Palace Result: {title[:70]}...') # Store as palace source construction_timeline['palace_sources'].append({ 'title': title, 'link': link, 'query': result['query'], 'snippet': snippet, 'years_mentioned': years, 'relevance_score': result['relevance_score'] }) # Extract construction dates if result['construction_mention'] and years: for year in years: construction_timeline['construction_dates'].append({ 'year': year, 'context': 'Construction reference', 'source': title, 'link': link, 'evidence': snippet[:300] }) print(f' ‚úÖ Construction dates found: {years}') # Extract completion information combined_text = f'{title.lower()} {snippet.lower()}' if any(term in combined_text for term in ['completed', 'finished']) and years: for year in years: construction_timeline['completion_dates'].append({ 'year': year, 'context': 'Completion reference', 'source': title, 'link': link, 'evidence': snippet[:300] }) print(f' ‚úÖ Completion dates found: {years}') # Extract decorative period information if result['decoration_mention']: construction_timeline['decorative_periods'].append({ 'type': 'Decorative work reference', 'years_mentioned': years, 'source': title, 'link': link, 'evidence': snippet[:300] }) print(f' ‚úÖ Decorative work reference found') # Extract eight-year references if result['eight_years_mention']: construction_timeline['eight_year_references'].append({ 'context': 'Eight year period reference', 'years_mentioned': years, 'source': title, 'link': link, 'evidence': snippet[:300] }) print(f' ‚úÖ Eight-year reference found') # Save construction timeline analysis timeline_analysis_file = f'workspace/sheki_palace_FIXED_construction_analysis_{timestamp}.json' with open(timeline_analysis_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(construction_timeline, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print(f'\nüìÑ Construction timeline analysis saved to: {timeline_analysis_file}') # Display comprehensive findings print('\n\n' + '=' * 80) print('SHEKI KHAN\'S PALACE CONSTRUCTION TIMELINE RESEARCH RESULTS') print('=' * 80) print(f'\nüéØ PLAN OBJECTIVES STATUS:') if construction_timeline['construction_dates'] or construction_timeline['completion_dates']: all_construction_years = list(set([item['year'] for item in construction_timeline['construction_dates']] + [item['year'] for item in construction_timeline['completion_dates']])) print(f'‚úÖ Construction/Completion dates identified: {sorted(all_construction_years)}') else: print('‚ùå Construction/Completion dates: Not clearly identified') if construction_timeline['eight_year_references']: print(f'‚úÖ Eight-year decorative period: {len(construction_timeline["eight_year_references"])} references found') else: print('‚ùå Eight-year decorative period: Not clearly identified') if construction_timeline['decorative_periods']: print(f'‚úÖ Decorative work references: {len(construction_timeline["decorative_periods"])} found') else: print('‚ùå Decorative work references: Not found') print(f'\nüìä EVIDENCE STRENGTH:') print(f'‚Ä¢ Palace-specific sources: {len(construction_timeline["palace_sources"])}') print(f'‚Ä¢ Construction timeline evidence: {len(construction_timeline["construction_dates"])}') print(f'‚Ä¢ Completion timeline evidence: {len(construction_timeline["completion_dates"])}') print(f'‚Ä¢ Decorative period evidence: {len(construction_timeline["decorative_periods"])}') print(f'‚Ä¢ Eight-year period evidence: {len(construction_timeline["eight_year_references"])}') print(f'‚Ä¢ Results with specific years: {len(results_with_years)}') # Show most promising results with detailed evidence if palace_mentions: print(f'\nüèÜ PALACE-SPECIFIC RESULTS WITH CONSTRUCTION TIMELINE:') for i, result in enumerate(palace_mentions[:5], 1): # Show top 5 palace results print(f'\n{i}. {result["title"]}') print(f' Link: {result["link"]}') print(f' Years mentioned: {result["years_mentioned"]}') print(f' Relevance score: {result["relevance_score"]}') print(f' Key indicators: {result["matching_indicators"]}') print(f' Evidence: {result["snippet"][:250]}...') print('-' * 60) # Show year frequency analysis if available if construction_timeline['year_frequency']: print(f'\nüìÖ FINAL CONSTRUCTION YEAR ANALYSIS:') sorted_years = sorted(construction_timeline['year_frequency'].items(), key=lambda x: int(x[0])) for year, count in sorted_years: print(f'‚Ä¢ {year}: appears in {count} source(s) - {"LIKELY CONSTRUCTION DATE" if count >= 2 else "Single mention"}') print('\n‚úÖ FIXED SEARCH FOR SHEKI KHAN\'S PALACE CONSTRUCTION TIMELINE COMPLETED!') print('Construction timeline data successfully collected and analyzed from palace-specific sources.')

Store result with comprehensive analysis all_fresh_results.append({ 'search_number': i, 'query': query, 'result_number': j, 'title': title, 'link': link, 'snippet': snippet, 'relevance_score': relevance_score, 'matching_indicators': matching_indicators, 'years_mentioned': year_patterns, 'centuries_mentioned': century_patterns, 'palace_mention': any(term in combined_text for term in ['sheki', 'shaki', 'khan palace']), 'construction_mention': any(term in combined_text for term in ['construction', 'built', 'completed', 'finished']), 'decoration_mention': any(term in combined_text for term in ['decoration', 'decorative', 'embellishment']), 'eight_years_mention': 'eight years' in combined_text or '8 years' in combined_text, 'timeline_mention': any(term in combined_text for term in ['timeline', 'history', 'period', 'date']) }) print('-' * 40) else: print(f'‚ùå No results found for query {i}') failed_searches += 1 except Exception as e: print(f'‚ùå Error during search {i}: {str(e)}') failed_searches += 1 continue # Small delay between searches to avoid rate limiting time.sleep(1) print('\n' + '=' * 80) # Save comprehensive fresh search results timestamp = datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S') fresh_results_file = f'workspace/sheki_palace_FIXED_targeted_search_{timestamp}.json' search_data = { 'search_timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat(), 'search_purpose': 'FIXED targeted search for Palace of Shaki Khans construction timeline', 'research_objectives': [ 'Identify construction start date', 'Find completion date after eight-year decorative embellishment', 'Extract specific timeline for decorative work', 'Locate historical construction records for Palace of Shaki Khans' ], 'total_queries': len(targeted_queries), 'successful_searches': successful_searches, 'failed_searches': failed_searches, 'total_results': len(all_fresh_results), 'queries_executed': targeted_queries, 'results': all_fresh_results } with open(fresh_results_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(search_data, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print(f'\n\nüìä FIXED SEARCH EXECUTION SUMMARY:') print(f'Total queries executed: {len(targeted_queries)}') print(f'Successful searches: {successful_searches}') print(f'Failed searches: {failed_searches}') print(f'Total results collected: {len(all_fresh_results)}') print(f'Fixed search results saved to: {fresh_results_file}') # Immediate analysis of SUCCESSFULLY collected results print('\n\nüîç ANALYSIS OF SUCCESSFULLY COLLECTED CONSTRUCTION TIMELINE DATA:') print('=' * 75) # Filter results by relevance and specific content high_relevance_results = [r for r in all_fresh_results if r['relevance_score'] >= 4] palace_mentions = [r for r in all_fresh_results if r['palace_mention']] construction_mentions = [r for r in all_fresh_results if r['construction_mention']] decoration_mentions = [r for r in all_fresh_results if r['decoration_mention']] eight_years_mentions = [r for r in all_fresh_results if r['eight_years_mention']] results_with_years = [r for r in all_fresh_results if r['years_mentioned']] print(f'\nüìã FIXED RESULT CATEGORIZATION:') print(f'High relevance results (4+ indicators): {len(high_relevance_results)}') print(f'Results mentioning Palace/Sheki/Shaki: {len(palace_mentions)}') print(f'Results with construction references: {len(construction_mentions)}') print(f'Results with decoration references: {len(decoration_mentions)}') print(f'Results mentioning eight years: {len(eight_years_mentions)}') print(f'Results containing specific years: {len(results_with_years)}') # Extract and analyze construction timeline information print('\n\nüèóÔ∏è CONSTRUCTION TIMELINE EXTRACTION FROM COLLECTED DATA:') print('=' * 60) construction_timeline = { 'construction_dates': [], 'completion_dates': [], 'decorative_periods': [], 'eight_year_references': [], 'palace_sources': [], 'year_frequency': {} } # Collect all years mentioned across palace-related results all_years_mentioned = [] for result in palace_mentions: all_years_mentioned.extend(result['years_mentioned']) if all_years_mentioned: year_frequency = Counter(all_years_mentioned) construction_timeline['year_frequency'] = dict(year_frequency) print(f'üìÖ CONSTRUCTION YEAR FREQUENCY ANALYSIS:') print('-' * 40) for year, count in year_frequency.most_common(): print(f'‚Ä¢ {year}: mentioned {count} time(s)') # Analyze palace results for specific timeline information for result in palace_mentions: title = result['title'] snippet = result['snippet'] link = result['link'] years = result['years_mentioned'] print(f'\nüè∞ Analyzing Palace Result: {title[:70]}...') # Store as palace source construction_timeline['palace_sources'].append({ 'title': title, 'link': link, 'query': result['query'], 'snippet': snippet, 'years_mentioned': years, 'relevance_score': result['relevance_score'] }) # Extract construction dates if result['construction_mention'] and years: for year in years: construction_timeline['construction_dates'].append({ 'year': year, 'context': 'Construction reference', 'source': title, 'link': link, 'evidence': snippet[:300] }) print(f' ‚úÖ Construction dates found: {years}') # Extract completion information combined_text = f'{title.lower()} {snippet.lower()}' if any(term in combined_text for term in ['completed', 'finished']) and years: for year in years: construction_timeline['completion_dates'].append({ 'year': year, 'context': 'Completion reference', 'source': title, 'link': link, 'evidence': snippet[:300] }) print(f' ‚úÖ Completion dates found: {years}') # Extract decorative period information if result['decoration_mention']: construction_timeline['decorative_periods'].append({ 'type': 'Decorative work reference', 'years_mentioned': years, 'source': title, 'link': link, 'evidence': snippet[:300] }) print(f' ‚úÖ Decorative work reference found') # Extract eight-year references if result['eight_years_mention']: construction_timeline['eight_year_references'].append({ 'context': 'Eight year period reference', 'years_mentioned': years, 'source': title, 'link': link, 'evidence': snippet[:300] }) print(f' ‚úÖ Eight-year reference found') # Save construction timeline analysis timeline_analysis_file = f'workspace/sheki_palace_FIXED_construction_analysis_{timestamp}.json' with open(timeline_analysis_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(construction_timeline, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print(f'\nüìÑ Construction timeline analysis saved to: {timeline_analysis_file}') # Display comprehensive findings print('\n\n' + '=' * 80) print('SHEKI KHAN\'S PALACE CONSTRUCTION TIMELINE RESEARCH RESULTS') print('=' * 80) print(f'\nüéØ PLAN OBJECTIVES STATUS:') if construction_timeline['construction_dates'] or construction_timeline['completion_dates']: all_construction_years = list(set([item['year'] for item in construction_timeline['construction_dates']] + [item['year'] for item in construction_timeline['completion_dates']])) print(f'‚úÖ Construction/Completion dates identified: {sorted(all_construction_years)}') else: print('‚ùå Construction/Completion dates: Not clearly identified') if construction_timeline['eight_year_references']: print(f'‚úÖ Eight-year decorative period: {len(construction_timeline["eight_year_references"])} references found') else: print('‚ùå Eight-year decorative period: Not clearly identified') if construction_timeline['decorative_periods']: print(f'‚úÖ Decorative work references: {len(construction_timeline["decorative_periods"])} found') else: print('‚ùå Decorative work references: Not found') print(f'\nüìä EVIDENCE STRENGTH:') print(f'‚Ä¢ Palace-specific sources: {len(construction_timeline["palace_sources"])}') print(f'‚Ä¢ Construction timeline evidence: {len(construction_timeline["construction_dates"])}') print(f'‚Ä¢ Completion timeline evidence: {len(construction_timeline["completion_dates"])}') print(f'‚Ä¢ Decorative period evidence: {len(construction_timeline["decorative_periods"])}') print(f'‚Ä¢ Eight-year period evidence: {len(construction_timeline["eight_year_references"])}') print(f'‚Ä¢ Results with specific years: {len(results_with_years)}') # from ddgs import DDGS import json import os from datetime import datetime import time import re from collections import Counter # Create workspace directory if it doesn't exist if not os.path.exists('workspace'): os.makedirs('workspace') print('Created workspace directory') # Execute targeted search with PROPERLY ORDERED variable definitions print('=== PROPERLY FIXED SEARCH FOR SHEKI KHAN\'S PALACE CONSTRUCTION TIMELINE ===') print('Goal: Find construction dates and eight-year decorative embellishment timeline') print('Focus: Palace of Shaki Khans with CORRECT variable definition order') print('=' * 80) # Define targeted search queries for Palace of Shaki Khans targeted_queries = [ 'Palace of Shaki Khans construction 1797 1762 Azerbaijan', 'Sheki Khan Palace built completed construction history', 'Azerbaijan Shaki Palace construction eight years decoration', 'Palace Shaki Khans building timeline decorative work', 'Sheki Khan Palace construction period 18th century Muhammad Husayn Khan' ] print(f'Starting search with {len(targeted_queries)} targeted queries...') print('Collecting construction timeline information for Palace of Shaki Khans') print('=' * 80) # Initialize search and storage searcher = DDGS(timeout=15) all_results = [] successful_searches = 0 failed_searches = 0 # Execute searches with FIXED processing logic for i, query in enumerate(targeted_queries, 1): print(f'\nSearch {i}/{len(targeted_queries)}: {query}') print('-' * 70) try: # Initialize search and storage searcher = DDGS(timeout=15) all_results = [] successful_searches = 0 failed_searches = 0 # Execute searches with FIXED processing logic for i, query in enumerate(targeted_queries, 1): print(f'\nSearch {i}/{len(targeted_queries)}: {query}') print('-' * 70) try: # Perform search results = searcher.text( query, max_results=10, page=1, backend=["google", "duckduckgo", "bing"], safesearch="off", region="en-us" ) if results: print(f'‚úÖ Found {len(results)} results for query {i}') successful_searches += 1 # Now analyze with properly defined combined_text palace_indicators = [ 'sheki', 'shaki', 'khan palace', 'palace of shaki khans', 'palace of sheki khans', 'azerbaijan', 'construction', 'built', 'completed', 'decoration', 'decorative', 'embellishment' ] matching_indicators = [indicator for indicator in palace_indicators if indicator in combined_text] relevance_score = len(matching_indicators) # Extract construction timeline information print('\n\nüèóÔ∏è CONSTRUCTION TIMELINE EXTRACTION:') print('=' * 45) construction_timeline = { 'construction_dates': [], 'completion_dates': [], 'decorative_periods': [], 'eight_year_references': [], 'palace_sources': [], 'year_frequency': {} } # Collect all years mentioned in palace-related results all_years_mentioned = [] for result in palace_mentions: all_years_mentioned.extend(result['years_mentioned']) if all_years_mentioned: year_frequency = Counter(all_years_mentioned) construction_timeline['year_frequency'] = dict(year_frequency) print(f'üìÖ CONSTRUCTION YEAR FREQUENCY ANALYSIS:') print('-' * 40) for year, count in year_frequency.most_common(): print(f'‚Ä¢ {year}: mentioned {count} time(s)') # Analyze each palace result for timeline information for result in palace_mentions: title = result['title'] snippet = result['snippet'] link = result['link'] years = result['years_mentioned'] print(f'\nüè∞ Analyzing Palace Result: {title[:70]}...') # Store as palace source construction_timeline['palace_sources'].append({ 'title': title, 'link': link, 'query': result['query'], 'snippet': snippet, 'years_mentioned': years, 'relevance_score': result['relevance_score'] }) # Extract construction dates if result['construction_mention'] and years: for year in years: construction_timeline['construction_dates'].append({ 'year': year, 'context': 'Construction reference', 'source': title, 'link': link, 'evidence': snippet[:300] }) print(f' ‚úÖ Construction dates found: {years}') # Extract completion information combined_text = f'{title.lower()} {snippet.lower()}' if any(term in combined_text for term in ['completed', 'finished']) and years: for year in years: construction_timeline['completion_dates'].append({ 'year': year, 'context': 'Completion reference', 'source': title, 'link': link, 'evidence': snippet[:300] }) print(f' ‚úÖ Completion dates found: {years}') # Extract decorative period information if result['decoration_mention']: construction_timeline['decorative_periods'].append({ 'type': 'Decorative work reference', 'years_mentioned': years, 'source': title, 'link': link, 'evidence': snippet[:300] }) print(f' ‚úÖ Decorative work reference found') # Save timeline analysis timeline_file = f'workspace/sheki_palace_construction_timeline_analysis_{timestamp}.json' with open(timeline_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(construction_timeline, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print(f'\nüìÑ Construction timeline analysis saved to: {timeline_file}') # Perform search results = searcher.text( query, max_results=10, page=1, backend=["google", "duckduckgo", "bing"], safesearch="off", region="en-us" ) if results: print(f'‚úÖ Found {len(results)} results for query {i}') successful_searches += 1 # RESTRUCTURED: Create a separate function to analyze each result def analyze_result(title, snippet, link): """Analyze a single search result for palace construction timeline information""" # Define combined_text at the start of analysis function combined_text = f'{title.lower()} {snippet.lower()}' # Define indicators palace_indicators = [ 'sheki', 'shaki', 'khan palace', 'palace of shaki khans', 'palace of sheki khans', 'azerbaijan', 'construction', 'built', 'completed', 'decoration', 'decorative', 'embellishment' ] # Find matching indicators matching_indicators = [indicator for indicator in palace_indicators if indicator in combined_text] relevance_score = len(matching_indicators) # Extract years year_patterns = re.findall(r'\b(1[6-9]\d{2}|20\d{2})\b', combined_text) century_patterns = re.findall(r'\b(\d{1,2})(th|st|nd|rd)\s+century\b', combined_text) # Analyze specific features palace_mention = any(term in combined_text for term in ['sheki', 'shaki', 'khan palace']) construction_mention = any(term in combined_text for term in ['construction', 'built', 'completed', 'finished']) decoration_mention = any(term in combined_text for term in ['decoration', 'decorative', 'embellishment']) eight_years_mention = 'eight years' in combined_text or '8 years' in combined_text timeline_mention = any(term in combined_text for term in ['timeline', 'history', 'period', 'date']) return { 'relevance_score': relevance_score, 'matching_indicators': matching_indicators, 'years_mentioned': year_patterns, 'centuries_mentioned': century_patterns, 'palace_mention': palace_mention, 'construction_mention': construction_mention, 'decoration_mention': decoration_mention, 'eight_years_mention': eight_years_mention, 'timeline_mention': timeline_mention } # Call analysis function analysis = analyze_result(title, snippet, link) # Display analysis results if analysis['relevance_score'] >= 3: print(f'üéØ HIGH RELEVANCE ({analysis["relevance_score"]} indicators): {analysis["matching_indicators"]}') if analysis['palace_mention']: print('üè∞ PALACE MATCH: Contains Sheki/Shaki Khan Palace reference') if analysis['construction_mention']: print('üèóÔ∏è CONSTRUCTION: Contains construction timeline reference') if analysis['decoration_mention']: print('üé® DECORATION: Contains decorative work reference') if analysis['eight_years_mention']: print('‚è∞ EIGHT YEARS: Contains eight-year reference') if analysis['years_mentioned']: print(f'üìÖ YEARS FOUND: {analysis["years_mentioned"]}') if analysis['centuries_mentioned']: print(f'üìÖ CENTURIES FOUND: {analysis["centuries_mentioned"]}') elif analysis['relevance_score'] >= 1: print(f'‚≠ê RELEVANT ({analysis["relevance_score"]} indicators): {analysis["matching_indicators"]}') if analysis['years_mentioned']: print(f'üìÖ Years mentioned: {analysis["years_mentioned"]}') # Store result with all analysis data result_data = { 'search_number': i, 'query': query, 'result_number': j, 'title': title, 'link': link, 'snippet': snippet } result_data.update(analysis) # Add analysis results all_results.append(result_data) print('-' * 40) else: print(f'‚ùå No results found for query {i}') failed_searches += 1 except Exception as e: print(f'‚ùå Error during search {i}: {str(e)}') failed_searches += 1 continue time.sleep(1) print('\n' + '=' * 80) # Extract construction timeline information print('\n\nüèóÔ∏è CONSTRUCTION TIMELINE EXTRACTION:') print('=' * 45) construction_timeline = { 'construction_dates': [], 'completion_dates': [], 'decorative_periods': [], 'eight_year_references': [], 'palace_sources': [], 'year_frequency': {} } # Collect all years mentioned in palace-related results all_years_mentioned = [] for result in palace_mentions: all_years_mentioned.extend(result['years_mentioned']) if all_years_mentioned: year_frequency = Counter(all_years_mentioned) construction_timeline['year_frequency'] = dict(year_frequency) print(f'üìÖ CONSTRUCTION YEAR FREQUENCY ANALYSIS:') print('-' * 40) for year, count in year_frequency.most_common(): print(f'‚Ä¢ {year}: mentioned {count} time(s)') # Analyze each palace result for timeline information for result in palace_mentions: title = result['title'] snippet = result['snippet'] link = result['link'] years = result['years_mentioned'] print(f'\nüè∞ Analyzing Palace Result: {title[:70]}...') # Store as palace source construction_timeline['palace_sources'].append({ 'title': title, 'link': link, 'query': result['query'], 'snippet': snippet, 'years_mentioned': years, 'relevance_score': result['relevance_score'] }) # Extract construction dates if result['construction_mention'] and years: for year in years: construction_timeline['construction_dates'].append({ 'year': year, 'context': 'Construction reference', 'source': title, 'link': link, 'evidence': snippet[:300] }) print(f' ‚úÖ Construction dates found: {years}') # Call analysis function analysis = analyze_result(title, snippet, link) # Display analysis results if analysis['relevance_score'] >= 3: print(f'üéØ HIGH RELEVANCE ({analysis["relevance_score"]} indicators): {analysis["matching_indicators"]}') if analysis['palace_mention']: print('üè∞ PALACE MATCH: Contains Sheki/Shaki Khan Palace reference') if analysis['construction_mention']: print('üèóÔ∏è CONSTRUCTION: Contains construction timeline reference') if analysis['decoration_mention']: print('üé® DECORATION: Contains decorative work reference') if analysis['eight_years_mention']: print('‚è∞ EIGHT YEARS: Contains eight-year reference') if analysis['years_mentioned']: print(f'üìÖ YEARS FOUND: {analysis["years_mentioned"]}') if analysis['centuries_mentioned']: print(f'üìÖ CENTURIES FOUND: {analysis["centuries_mentioned"]}') elif analysis['relevance_score'] >= 1: print(f'‚≠ê RELEVANT ({analysis["relevance_score"]} indicators): {analysis["matching_indicators"]}') if analysis['years_mentioned']: print(f'üìÖ Years mentioned: {analysis["years_mentioned"]}') # Store result with all analysis data result_data = { 'search_number': i, 'query': query, 'result_number': j, 'title': title, 'link': link, 'snippet': snippet } result_data.update(analysis) # Add analysis results all_results.append(result_data) print('-' * 40) else: print(f'‚ùå No results found for query {i}') failed_searches += 1 except Exception as e: print(f'‚ùå Error during search {i}: {str(e)}') failed_searches += 1 continue time.sleep(1) print('\n' + '=' * 80) # Save search results timestamp = datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S') results_file = f'workspace/sheki_palace_restructured_search_{timestamp}.json' search_data = { 'search_timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat(), 'search_purpose': 'Restructured search for Palace of Shaki Khans construction timeline', 'research_objectives': [ 'Identify construction start date', 'Find completion date after eight-year decorative embellishment', 'Extract specific timeline for decorative work', 'Locate historical construction records' ], 'total_queries': len(targeted_queries), 'successful_searches': successful_searches, 'failed_searches': failed_searches, 'total_results': len(all_results), 'queries_executed': targeted_queries, 'results': all_results } with open(results_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(search_data, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print(f'\n\nüìä SEARCH EXECUTION SUMMARY:') print(f'Total queries executed: {len(targeted_queries)}') print(f'Successful searches: {successful_searches}') print(f'Failed searches: {failed_searches}') print(f'Total results collected: {len(all_results)}') print(f'Search results saved to: {results_file}') # Analyze collected results print('\n\nüîç CONSTRUCTION TIMELINE DATA ANALYSIS:') print('=' * 50) # Filter results by categories high_relevance_results = [r for r in all_results if r['relevance_score'] >= 4] palace_mentions = [r for r in all_results if r['palace_mention']] construction_mentions = [r for r in all_results if r['construction_mention']] decoration_mentions = [r for r in all_results if r['decoration_mention']] eight_years_mentions = [r for r in all_results if r['eight_years_mention']] results_with_years = [r for r in all_results if r['years_mentioned']] print(f'\nüìã RESULT CATEGORIZATION:') print(f'High relevance results (4+ indicators): {len(high_relevance_results)}') print(f'Results mentioning Palace/Sheki/Shaki: {len(palace_mentions)}') print(f'Results with construction references: {len(construction_mentions)}') print(f'Results with decoration references: {len(decoration_mentions)}') print(f'Results mentioning eight years: {len(eight_years_mentions)}') print(f'Results containing specific years: {len(results_with_years)}') # Extract construction timeline information print('\n\nüèóÔ∏è CONSTRUCTION TIMELINE EXTRACTION:') print('=' * 45) construction_timeline = { 'construction_dates': [], 'completion_dates': [], 'decorative_periods': [], 'eight_year_references': [], 'palace_sources': [], 'year_frequency': {} } # Collect all years mentioned in palace-related results all_years_mentioned = [] for result in palace_mentions: all_years_mentioned.extend(result['years_mentioned']) if all_years_mentioned: year_frequency = Counter(all_years_mentioned) construction_timeline['year_frequency'] = dict(year_frequency) print(f'üìÖ CONSTRUCTION YEAR FREQUENCY ANALYSIS:') print('-' * 40) for year, count in year_frequency.most_common(): print(f'‚Ä¢ {year}: mentioned {count} time(s)') # Analyze each palace result for timeline information for result in palace_mentions: title = result['title'] snippet = result['snippet'] link = result['link'] years = result['years_mentioned'] print(f'\nüè∞ Analyzing Palace Result: {title[:70]}...') # Store as palace source construction_timeline['palace_sources'].append({ 'title': title, 'link': link, 'query': result['query'], 'snippet': snippet, 'years_mentioned': years, 'relevance_score': result['relevance_score'] }) # Extract construction dates if result['construction_mention'] and years: for year in years: construction_timeline['construction_dates'].append({ 'year': year, 'context': 'Construction reference', 'source': title, 'link': link, 'evidence': snippet[:300] }) print(f' ‚úÖ Construction dates found: {years}') # Extract completion information combined_text = f'{title.lower()} {snippet.lower()}' if any(term in combined_text for term in ['completed', 'finished']) and years: for year in years: construction_timeline['completion_dates'].append({ 'year': year, 'context': 'Completion reference', 'source': title, 'link': link, 'evidence': snippet[:300] }) print(f' ‚úÖ Completion dates found: {years}') # Extract decorative period information if result['decoration_mention']: construction_timeline['decorative_periods'].append({ 'type': 'Decorative work reference', 'years_mentioned': years, 'source': title, 'link': link, 'evidence': snippet[:300] }) print(f' ‚úÖ Decorative work reference found') # Extract eight-year references if result['eight_years_mention']: construction_timeline['eight_year_references'].append({ 'context': 'Eight year period reference', 'years_mentioned': years, 'source': title, 'link': link, 'evidence': snippet[:300] }) print(f' ‚úÖ Eight-year reference found') # Save timeline analysis timeline_file = f'workspace/sheki_palace_construction_timeline_final_{timestamp}.json' with open(timeline_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(construction_timeline, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) print(f'\nüìÑ Construction timeline analysis saved to: {timeline_file}') # Display final results print('\n\n' + '=' * 80) print('SHEKI KHAN\'S PALACE CONSTRUCTION TIMELINE RESEARCH RESULTS') print('=' * 80) print(f'\nüéØ PLAN OBJECTIVES STATUS:') if construction_timeline['construction_dates'] or construction_timeline['completion_dates']: all_construction_years = list(set([item['year'] for item in construction_timeline['construction_dates']] + [item['year'] for item in construction_timeline['completion_dates']])) print(f'‚úÖ Construction/Completion dates identified: {sorted(all_construction_years)}') else: print('‚ùå Construction/Completion dates: Not clearly identified') if construction_timeline['eight_year_references']: print(f'‚úÖ Eight-year decorative period: {len(construction_timeline["eight_year_references"])} references found') else: print('‚ùå Eight-year decorative period: Not clearly identified') if construction_timeline['decorative_periods']: print(f'‚úÖ Decorative work references: {len(construction_timeline["decorative_periods"])} found') else: print('‚ùå Decorative work references: Not found') print(f'\nüìä EVIDENCE STRENGTH:') print(f'‚Ä¢ Palace-specific sources: {len(construction_timeline["palace_sources"])}') print(f'‚Ä¢ Construction timeline evidence: {len(construction_timeline["construction_dates"])}') print(f'‚Ä¢ Completion timeline evidence: {len(construction_timeline["completion_dates"])}') print(f'‚Ä¢ Decorative period evidence: {len(construction_timeline["decorative_periods"])}') print(f'‚Ä¢ Eight-year period evidence: {len(construction_timeline["eight_year_references"])}') print(f'‚Ä¢ Results with specific years: {len(results_with_years)}') #
